----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: client/services/chat/components/ChatBox.jsx
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ChatBox.jsx
import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect, useMemo } from "react";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";
import PropTypes from "prop-types";
import { fetchWithAuth } from "@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth";
import { translateMessageToEnglish } from "@/shared/utils/translateMessage";
import { toast } from "react-toastify";
import ConversationList from "./ConversationList";
import ForwardChatModal from "./ForwardChatModal";
import EmojiPicker from "./EmojiPicker";
import {
  Paperclip,
  Camera,
  SendHorizontal,
  Star,
  Reply,
  Forward,
  X,
  Link2,
  AtSign,
  ChevronDown,
  Languages,
  MoreVertical,
  Smile,
  Image as ImageIcon,
  Hash,
  GripHorizontal,
} from "lucide-react";

const TONE_CHIPS = [
  { label: "Friendly", prefix: "Hey! " },
  { label: "Urgent", prefix: "⚠️ " },
  { label: "Thankful", prefix: "Thanks so much! " },
  { label: "Funny", prefix: "😂 " },
  { label: "Clear", prefix: "Just to clarify, " },
];

const ALL_MENTION_OPTION = {
  id: "__mention_all__",
  username: "all",
  label: "Everyone in this chatroom",
  isAllMention: true,
};

const convertHtmlAnchorsToMarkdown = (content = "") => {
  if (typeof content !== "string" || !content) {
    return "";
  }

  return content.replace(
    /<a\s+[^>]*href=["']([^"']+)["'][^>]*>(.*?)<\/a>/gi,
    (_, href, label) => {
      const cleanLabel = String(label || "")
        .replace(/<[^>]*>/g, "")
        .trim() || href;

      return `[${cleanLabel}](${href})`;
    }
  );
};

const stripHtmlTags = (value = "") =>
  String(value)
    .replace(/<br\s*\/?>/gi, "\n")
    .replace(/<[^>]*>/g, "")
    .trim();

const buildChatUrl = (chat) => {
  const chatRoomId = chat?.chatRoomId || chat?.chatRoom?.id || chat?.thread?.chatRoomId;
  const threadId = chat?.threadId || chat?.thread?.id;
  const messageId = chat?.id;

  if (!chatRoomId || !threadId || !messageId) {
    return "";
  }

  if (typeof window === "undefined") {
    return `/chat?chatRoomId=${encodeURIComponent(chatRoomId)}&threadId=${encodeURIComponent(threadId)}&messageId=${encodeURIComponent(messageId)}`;
  }

  const url = new URL("/chat", window.location.origin);
  url.searchParams.set("chatRoomId", chatRoomId);
  url.searchParams.set("threadId", threadId);
  url.searchParams.set("messageId", messageId);

  return url.toString();
};

const buildContextSnippet = (chat) => {
  const snippet = stripHtmlTags(chat?.contentHtml || chat?.content || "");
  if (!snippet) return "Message";
  return snippet.length > 180 ? `${snippet.slice(0, 180)}…` : snippet;
};

const buildReplyMessageWithContext = (message, actionContext) => {
  if (!actionContext?.chat) {
    return message;
  }

  const chat = actionContext.chat;
  const chatUrl = buildChatUrl(chat);
  const sender = chat?.sender?.username || "Unknown";
  const roomName = chat?.chatRoom?.name || "Unknown room";
  const sentAtRaw = chat?.updatedAt || chat?.createdAt || "";
  const sentAt = sentAtRaw ? new Date(sentAtRaw).toLocaleString() : "";
  const originalMessage = stripHtmlTags(chat?.contentHtml || chat?.content || "") || "Original message";

  const lines = [];

  if (String(message || "").trim()) {
    lines.push(String(message).trim(), "");
  }

  lines.push("Replying to message");
  lines.push(`Sender: ${sender}`);
  lines.push(`Chat Room: ${roomName}`);

  if (sentAt) {
    lines.push(`Sent: ${sentAt}`);
  }

  if (chatUrl) {
    lines.push(`Link: [Open original message](${chatUrl})`);
  }

  lines.push("Original message:");
  lines.push(originalMessage);

  return lines.join("\n");
};

const ChatBox = ({
  conversationHistory,
  onUpdateConversation,
  onSendMessage,
  currentUserId,
  onDeleteChat,
  onPinChat,
  onOpenDirectMessage,
  userRole,
  scrollToMessageId,
  selectedThread,
  chatRoomId,
}) => {
  const [message, setMessage] = useState("");
  const [attachments, setAttachments] = useState([]);
  const [isImportant, setIsImportant] = useState(false);
  const [messageAction, setMessageAction] = useState(null);
  const [forwardChat, setForwardChat] = useState(null);
  const [mentionUsers, setMentionUsers] = useState([]);
  const [translating, setTranslating] = useState(false);
  const [mentionQuery, setMentionQuery] = useState(null);
  const [dismissedTaggedChatIds, setDismissedTaggedChatIds] = useState([]);
  const [activeTaggedIndex, setActiveTaggedIndex] = useState(0);
  const [taggedScrollTarget, setTaggedScrollTarget] = useState(null);
  const [taggedScrollRequestToken, setTaggedScrollRequestToken] = useState(0);
  const [showMoreMenu, setShowMoreMenu] = useState(false);
  const [showEmojiPicker, setShowEmojiPicker] = useState(false);
  const [showToneChips, setShowToneChips] = useState(false);
  const [showGifPicker, setShowGifPicker] = useState(false);
  const [gifSearchResults, setGifSearchResults] = useState([]);
  const [gifSearchQuery, setGifSearchQuery] = useState("");
  const [gifSearchLoading, setGifSearchLoading] = useState(false);
  const moreMenuRef = useRef(null);
  const emojiPickerRef = useRef(null);
  const toneChipsRef = useRef(null);
  const textareaRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleClickOutside = (e) => {
      if (moreMenuRef.current && !moreMenuRef.current.contains(e.target)) {
        setShowMoreMenu(false);
      }
      if (emojiPickerRef.current && !emojiPickerRef.current.contains(e.target)) {
        setShowEmojiPicker(false);
      }
      if (toneChipsRef.current && !toneChipsRef.current.contains(e.target)) {
        setShowToneChips(false);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
  }, []);

  const taggedDismissalsKey = useMemo(
    () => `chat-tag-dismissals:${currentUserId || "unknown"}:${selectedThread || "no-thread"}`,
    [currentUserId, selectedThread]
  );

  const normalizedConversationHistory = useMemo(
    () =>
      (Array.isArray(conversationHistory) ? conversationHistory : []).map((chat) => {
        if (!chat || typeof chat !== "object") {
          return chat;
        }

        const originalContent = typeof chat.content === "string" ? chat.content : "";
        const normalizedContent = convertHtmlAnchorsToMarkdown(originalContent);

        return {
          ...chat,
          content: normalizedContent,
          contentHtml: originalContent,
          containsHtmlLinks: /<a\s+[^>]*href=/i.test(originalContent),
        };
      }),
    [conversationHistory]
  );

  useEffect(() => {
    if (textareaRef.current) {
      textareaRef.current.focus();
      handleInput();
    }
  }, [messageAction]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (typeof window === "undefined") return;

    try {
      const stored = window.localStorage.getItem(taggedDismissalsKey);
      const parsed = stored ? JSON.parse(stored) : [];
      setDismissedTaggedChatIds(Array.isArray(parsed) ? parsed : []);
      setActiveTaggedIndex(0);
      setTaggedScrollTarget(null);
      setTaggedScrollRequestToken(0);
    } catch {
      setDismissedTaggedChatIds([]);
    }
  }, [taggedDismissalsKey]);

  useEffect(() => {
    let isMounted = true;

    const fetchMentionUsers = async () => {
      if (!chatRoomId) {
        setMentionUsers([]);
        return;
      }

      try {
        const res = await fetchWithAuth(
          `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chatrooms/${chatRoomId}/mention-users`
        );

        if (!res.ok) {
          return;
        }

        const data = await res.json();
        const allowedUsers = Array.isArray(data.users) ? data.users : [];

        if (isMounted) {
          setMentionUsers(
            allowedUsers.filter((user) => user.username && user.active !== false)
          );
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Fetch mention users error:", error);
      }
    };

    fetchMentionUsers();

    return () => {
      isMounted = false;
    };
  }, [chatRoomId]);

  const updateMentionQuery = (value, cursorPosition) => {
    const textBeforeCursor = String(value).slice(0, cursorPosition);
    const match = textBeforeCursor.match(/(^|[\s([{:;,])@([A-Za-z0-9_.-]{0,31})$/);

    if (!match) {
      setMentionQuery(null);
      return;
    }

    setMentionQuery({
      query: match[2].toLowerCase(),
      start: cursorPosition - match[2].length - 1,
      end: cursorPosition,
    });
  };

  const handleMessageChange = (e) => {
    const nextValue = e.target.value;
    setMessage(nextValue);
    updateMentionQuery(nextValue, e.target.selectionStart || nextValue.length);
  };

  const filteredMentionUsers = useMemo(() => {
    if (!mentionQuery) return [];

    const matchingUsers = mentionUsers
      .filter((user) => {
        const username = String(user.username || "").toLowerCase();
        return username && username.includes(mentionQuery.query);
      })
      .slice(0, 6);

    if ("all".includes(mentionQuery.query)) {
      return [ALL_MENTION_OPTION, ...matchingUsers].slice(0, 6);
    }

    return matchingUsers;
  }, [mentionQuery, mentionUsers]);

  const taggedChats = useMemo(() => {
    const dismissed = new Set(dismissedTaggedChatIds);

    return normalizedConversationHistory.filter((chat) => {
      if (!chat?.id || dismissed.has(chat.id)) return false;

      const tags = Array.isArray(chat.taggedUsers) ? chat.taggedUsers : [];
      return tags.some((tag) => tag?.userId === currentUserId || tag?.user?.id === currentUserId);
    });
  }, [currentUserId, dismissedTaggedChatIds, normalizedConversationHistory]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeTaggedIndex > taggedChats.length - 1) {
      setActiveTaggedIndex(0);
    }
  }, [activeTaggedIndex, taggedChats.length]);

  const activeTaggedChat = taggedChats[activeTaggedIndex] || null;
  const activeTaggedSnippet = activeTaggedChat ? buildContextSnippet(activeTaggedChat) : "";

  const persistDismissedTaggedChatIds = (nextIds) => {
    setDismissedTaggedChatIds(nextIds);

    if (typeof window === "undefined") return;

    try {
      window.localStorage.setItem(taggedDismissalsKey, JSON.stringify(nextIds));
    } catch {
      // Local storage can be unavailable in private modes; the in-memory state still works.
    }
  };

  const viewTaggedChat = (chat = activeTaggedChat) => {
    if (!chat?.id) return;
    setTaggedScrollTarget(chat.id);
    setTaggedScrollRequestToken((token) => token + 1);
  };

  const showNextTaggedChat = () => {
    if (taggedChats.length === 0) return;

    const nextIndex = (activeTaggedIndex + 1) % taggedChats.length;
    setActiveTaggedIndex(nextIndex);
    viewTaggedChat(taggedChats[nextIndex]);
  };

  const dismissTaggedChat = async (chat = activeTaggedChat) => {
    if (!chat?.id) return;
    persistDismissedTaggedChatIds([...new Set([...dismissedTaggedChatIds, chat.id])]);

    try {
      await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/widget/${chat.id}/dismiss`,
        { method: "PUT" }
      );
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Dismiss tagged chat error:", error);
    }
  };

  const insertMention = (user) => {
    if (!mentionQuery || !user?.username) return;

    const before = message.slice(0, mentionQuery.start);
    const after = message.slice(mentionQuery.end);
    const nextMessage = `${before}@${user.username} ${after}`;
    const nextCursor = before.length + user.username.length + 2;

    setMessage(nextMessage);
    setMentionQuery(null);

    window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      if (!textareaRef.current) return;
      textareaRef.current.focus();
      textareaRef.current.setSelectionRange(nextCursor, nextCursor);
      handleInput();
    });
  };

  const insertEmoji = (emoji) => {
    const textarea = textareaRef.current;
    if (!textarea) {
      setMessage((prev) => prev + emoji);
      return;
    }

    const start = textarea.selectionStart;
    const end = textarea.selectionEnd;
    const before = message.slice(0, start);
    const after = message.slice(end);
    const nextMessage = `${before}${emoji}${after}`;
    const nextCursor = start + emoji.length;

    setMessage(nextMessage);
    setShowEmojiPicker(false);

    window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      textarea.focus();
      textarea.setSelectionRange(nextCursor, nextCursor);
      handleInput();
    });
  };

  const applyToneChip = (tone) => {
    const textarea = textareaRef.current;
    if (!textarea) return;

    const start = textarea.selectionStart;
    const prefix = tone.prefix;
    const nextMessage = message.slice(0, start) + prefix + message.slice(start);
    const nextCursor = start + prefix.length;

    setMessage(nextMessage);
    setShowToneChips(false);

    window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      textarea.focus();
      textarea.setSelectionRange(nextCursor, nextCursor);
      handleInput();
    });
  };

  const searchGifs = async (query) => {
    if (!query.trim()) {
      setGifSearchResults([]);
      return;
    }

    setGifSearchLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/gifs/search?q=${encodeURIComponent(query.trim())}&limit=12`
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error("Failed to search GIFs");
      }
      const data = await res.json();
      setGifSearchResults(Array.isArray(data.gifs) ? data.gifs : []);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("GIF search error:", error);
      setGifSearchResults([]);
    } finally {
      setGifSearchLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const selectGif = (gif) => {
    const gifMarkdown = `![${gif.title || "GIF"}](${gif.url})`;
    const textarea = textareaRef.current;
    if (!textarea) {
      setMessage((prev) => prev + (prev ? "\n" : "") + gifMarkdown);
    } else {
      const start = textarea.selectionStart;
      const end = textarea.selectionEnd;
      const before = message.slice(0, start);
      const after = message.slice(end);
      const nextMessage = `${before}${gifMarkdown}${after}`;
      const nextCursor = start + gifMarkdown.length;
      setMessage(nextMessage);
      window.requestAnimationFrame(() => {
        textarea.focus();
        textarea.setSelectionRange(nextCursor, nextCursor);
        handleInput();
      });
    }
    setShowGifPicker(false);
    setGifSearchQuery("");
    setGifSearchResults([]);
  };

  const handleInput = () => {
    const textarea = textareaRef.current;
    if (textarea) {
      textarea.style.height = "auto";
      const maxHeight = 96;
      textarea.style.height = `${Math.min(textarea.scrollHeight, maxHeight)}px`;
    }
  };

  const handleKeyDown = (e) => {
    if (mentionQuery && filteredMentionUsers.length > 0) {
      if (e.key === "Tab") {
        e.preventDefault();
        insertMention(filteredMentionUsers[0]);
        return;
      }

      if (e.key === "Escape") {
        setMentionQuery(null);
        return;
      }
    }

    if (e.key === "Enter" && !e.shiftKey) {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleSubmit(e);
    }
  };

  const handleSubmit = (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();

    if (translating) return;

    if (message.trim() === "" && attachments.length === 0 && !messageAction) {
      return;
    }

    const payloadMessage = messageAction?.type === "reply"
      ? buildReplyMessageWithContext(message, messageAction)
      : message;

    onSendMessage(payloadMessage, attachments, isImportant);
    setMessage("");
    setAttachments([]);
    setIsImportant(false);
    setMessageAction(null);

    if (textareaRef.current) {
      textareaRef.current.style.height = "auto";
    }
  };

  const handleFileChange = (e) => {
    const files = Array.from(e.target.files);
    const allowedTypes = [
      "image/jpeg",
      "image/png",
      "image/gif",
      "video/mp4",
      "video/mpeg",
    ];
    const maxSize = 10 * 1024 * 1024;
    const validFiles = [];
    const errors = [];

    files.forEach((file) => {
      if (!allowedTypes.includes(file.type)) {
        errors.push(`${file.name}: File type not allowed. Only JPEG, PNG, GIF, MP4, MPEG.`);
      } else if (file.size > maxSize) {
        errors.push(`${file.name}: File too large (max 10MB).`);
      } else {
        validFiles.push(file);
      }
    });

    if (errors.length > 0) {
      errors.forEach((err) => toast.error(err));
    }

    if (validFiles.length > 0) {
      setAttachments((prev) => [...prev, ...validFiles]);
    }
  };

  const handleTranslateToEnglish = async () => {
    if (!message.trim()) {
      toast.error("Write a message to translate");
      return;
    }

    setTranslating(true);
    try {
      const translated = await translateMessageToEnglish({
        text: message,
        surface: "chat",
        format: "plain",
      });
      setMessage(translated || message);
      setMentionQuery(null);
      toast.success("Message translated to English");
      window.requestAnimationFrame(handleInput);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Translate chat error:", error);
      toast.error(error.message || "Failed to translate message");
    } finally {
      setTranslating(false);
    }
  };

  const markAsRead = async (chatId) => {
    if (!chatId) return;
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chats/${chatId}/read`,
        { method: "PUT" }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || "Failed to mark chat as read.");
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
      toast.error(error.message);
    }
  };

  const confirmRead = async (chatId) => {
    if (!chatId) return;
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chats/${chatId}/confirm`,
        { method: "PUT" }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || "Failed to confirm chat read.");
      }
      toast.success("Chat confirmed!");
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
      toast.error(error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleReplyToChat = (chat) => {
    setForwardChat(null);
    setMessageAction({ type: "reply", chat });
  };

  const handleForwardChat = (chat) => {
    setMessageAction(null);
    setForwardChat(chat);
  };

  const openOriginalMessage = () => {
    const chatUrl = buildChatUrl(messageAction?.chat);
    if (!chatUrl) return;
    window.location.assign(chatUrl);
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex h-full min-h-0 flex-col overflow-hidden">
      {activeTaggedChat && (
        <div className="overflow-hidden border-b border-[var(--color-brand-border)] bg-[var(--color-brand-light)] shadow-sm chat-fade-slide-in">
          <div className="px-4 py-2.5 text-[#312e81]">
            <div className="flex items-start gap-2 max-w-[var(--chat-timeline-max)] mx-auto">
              <div className="mt-0.5 flex h-8 w-8 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-[var(--color-brand)] text-white">
                <AtSign size={16} />
              </div>
              <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-semibold">
                  <span>You were tagged</span>
                  {taggedChats.length > 1 && (
                    <span className="rounded-full bg-[var(--color-brand-border)] px-2 py-0.5 text-xs">
                      {activeTaggedIndex + 1}/{taggedChats.length}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </div>
                <div className="mt-0.5 line-clamp-2 text-sm text-[#4338ca]/80">
                  {activeTaggedChat.sender?.username ? `${activeTaggedChat.sender.username}: ` : ""}
                  {activeTaggedSnippet}
                </div>
              </div>
              <div className="flex shrink-0 items-center gap-1">
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => viewTaggedChat()}
                  className="rounded-lg bg-[var(--color-brand)] px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold text-white hover:bg-[var(--color-brand-hover)] transition-colors"
                >
                  View
                </button>
                {taggedChats.length > 1 && (
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={showNextTaggedChat}
                    className="flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-lg hover:bg-white/50 text-[var(--color-brand)]"
                    aria-label="Next tagged message"
                    title="Next tagged message"
                  >
                    <ChevronDown size={16} />
                  </button>
                )}
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => dismissTaggedChat()}
                  className="flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-lg hover:bg-white/50 text-[var(--color-text-muted)]"
                  aria-label="Dismiss tagged message"
                  title="Dismiss tagged message"
                >
                  <X size={16} />
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
      <div className="flex-1 min-h-0 overflow-y-auto bg-[var(--color-surface)]">
        <ConversationList
          conversationHistory={normalizedConversationHistory}
          currentUserId={currentUserId}
          markAsRead={markAsRead}
          confirmRead={confirmRead}
          onDeleteChat={onDeleteChat}
          onPinChat={onPinChat}
          onReplyToChat={handleReplyToChat}
          onForwardChat={handleForwardChat}
          onOpenDirectMessage={onOpenDirectMessage}
          userRole={userRole}
          scrollToMessageId={taggedScrollTarget || scrollToMessageId}
          scrollToMessageRequestToken={taggedScrollRequestToken}
          selectedThread={selectedThread}
        />
      </div>

      {messageAction?.chat && (
        <div className="overflow-hidden border-t border-[var(--color-border)] bg-[var(--color-bg)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] chat-fade-slide-in">
          <div className="px-4 py-3">
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3 max-w-[var(--chat-timeline-max)] mx-auto">
              <div className="min-w-0">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--color-text-primary)]">
                  <Reply size={14} className="text-[var(--color-brand)]" />
                  <span>Replying to message</span>
                </div>
                <div className="mt-1 text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">
                  {messageAction.chat?.sender?.username || "Unknown"} • {messageAction.chat?.chatRoom?.name || "Unknown room"}
                </div>
                <div className="mt-1 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] whitespace-pre-wrap break-words line-clamp-2">
                  {buildContextSnippet(messageAction.chat)}
                </div>
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={openOriginalMessage}
                  className="mt-2 inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 text-xs text-[var(--color-brand)] hover:text-[var(--color-brand-hover)] font-medium"
                >
                  <Link2 size={12} />
                  Open original message
                </button>
              </div>

              <button
                type="button"
                onClick={() => setMessageAction(null)}
                className="flex h-7 w-7 items-center justify-center rounded-md hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] text-[var(--color-text-muted)]"
                title="Clear"
              >
                <X size={15} />
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      <div className="chat-composer">
        <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} className="chat-composer-inner">
          {filteredMentionUsers.length > 0 && (
            <div className="absolute bottom-full left-10 right-10 mb-2 max-h-64 overflow-y-auto rounded-lg border border-[var(--color-border)] bg-[var(--color-surface)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] shadow-lg sm:left-16 sm:right-auto sm:w-64">
              {filteredMentionUsers.map((user) => (
                <button
                  key={user.id}
                  type="button"
                  onMouseDown={(e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    insertMention(user);
                  }}
                  className="flex w-full flex-col px-3 py-2 text-left hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
                >
                  <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-[var(--color-brand)]">@{user.username}</span>
                  {user.isAllMention && (
                    <span className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">{user.label}</span>
                  )}
                  {(user.firstName || user.lastName) && (
                    <span className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">
                      {[user.firstName, user.lastName].filter(Boolean).join(" ")}
                    </span>
                  )}
                </button>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
          <input
            type="file"
            multiple
            accept="image/*,video/*"
            onChange={handleFileChange}
            className="hidden"
            id={`fileInput-${selectedThread}`}
          />
          <input
            type="file"
            accept="image/*"
            capture="environment"
            onChange={handleFileChange}
            className="hidden"
            id={`cameraInput-${selectedThread}`}
          />
          <textarea
            ref={textareaRef}
            value={message}
            onChange={handleMessageChange}
            onSelect={(e) => updateMentionQuery(e.target.value, e.target.selectionStart || 0)}
            onInput={handleInput}
            onKeyDown={handleKeyDown}
            placeholder={
              messageAction?.type === "reply"
                ? "Write your reply..."
                : "Type your message..."
            }
            className="min-w-0 flex-1 px-3 py-2.5 bg-transparent text-[var(--color-text-primary)] placeholder-[var(--color-text-muted)] resize-none focus:outline-none overscroll-contain text-sm leading-5"
            rows="1"
            style={{ maxHeight: "120px" }}
          />

          <div className="relative flex items-center" ref={moreMenuRef}>
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setShowMoreMenu((prev) => !prev)}
              className={`p-2 cursor-pointer rounded-lg transition-colors ${
                showMoreMenu
                  ? "text-[var(--color-text-primary)] bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
                  : "text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
              }`}
              title="More options"
              aria-label="More options"
            >
              <MoreVertical size={18} />
            </button>

            {showMoreMenu && (
              <div className="absolute bottom-full right-0 mb-2 bg-[var(--color-surface)] border border-[var(--color-border)] rounded-xl shadow-lg py-1 min-w-[180px] z-50">
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onMouseDown={(e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    document.getElementById(`fileInput-${selectedThread}`)?.click();
                    setShowMoreMenu(false);
                  }}
                  className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-primary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
                >
                  <Paperclip size={16} />
                  Attach files
                </button>
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onMouseDown={(e) => {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    document.getElementById(`cameraInput-${selectedThread}`)?.click();
                    setShowMoreMenu(false);
                  }}
                  className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-primary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
                >
                  <Camera size={16} />
                  Take photo
                </button>
                <div className="relative" ref={emojiPickerRef}>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => {
                      setShowToneChips(false);
                      setShowEmojiPicker((prev) => !prev);
                    }}
                    className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-primary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
                  >
                    <Smile size={16} />
                    Add emoji
                  </button>
                  {showEmojiPicker && (
                    <EmojiPicker
                      onSelect={insertEmoji}
                      onClose={() => setShowEmojiPicker(false)}
                      align="right"
                    />
                  )}
                </div>
                <div className="relative" ref={toneChipsRef}>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => {
                      setShowEmojiPicker(false);
                      setShowToneChips((prev) => !prev);
                    }}
                    className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-primary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
                  >
                    <GripHorizontal size={16} />
                    Tone helper
                  </button>
                  {showToneChips && (
                    <div className="absolute bottom-full right-0 mb-2 bg-[var(--color-surface)] border border-[var(--color-border)] rounded-xl shadow-lg py-1 min-w-[150px] z-50">
                      {TONE_CHIPS.map((tone) => (
                        <button
                          key={tone.label}
                          type="button"
                          onMouseDown={(e) => {
                            e.preventDefault();
                            applyToneChip(tone);
                            setShowMoreMenu(false);
                          }}
                          className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-primary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
                        >
                          {tone.prefix.match(/^.{1,2}/)?.[0] || "•"} {tone.label}
                        </button>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                  )}
                </div>
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => {
                    handleTranslateToEnglish();
                    setShowMoreMenu(false);
                  }}
                  disabled={translating || !message.trim()}
                  className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-primary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] disabled:text-[var(--color-text-muted)]"
                >
                  {translating ? (
                    <span className="loading loading-spinner loading-xs" />
                  ) : (
                    <Languages size={16} />
                  )}
                  Translate to English
                </button>
                <button
                  type="button"
                  onClick={() => {
                    setIsImportant((prev) => !prev);
                    setShowMoreMenu(false);
                  }}
                  aria-pressed={isImportant}
                  className="w-full flex items-center gap-2 px-3 py-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-primary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]"
                >
                  <Star size={16} className={isImportant ? "text-[var(--color-warning)] fill-current" : ""} />
                  Mark as important
                </button>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
          <motion.button
            type="submit"
            className={`flex items-center justify-center p-2.5 rounded-lg transition-all ${
              translating || (message.trim() === "" && attachments.length === 0 && !messageAction)
                ? "bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] text-[var(--color-text-muted)] cursor-not-allowed"
                : "bg-[var(--color-brand)] text-white hover:bg-[var(--color-brand-hover)] cursor-pointer shadow-sm"
            }`}
            disabled={translating || (message.trim() === "" && attachments.length === 0 && !messageAction)}
            aria-label="Send Message"
            whileHover={!(translating || (message.trim() === "" && attachments.length === 0 && !messageAction)) ? { scale: 1.08 } : {}}
            whileTap={{ scale: 0.9 }}
          >
            <SendHorizontal size={18} />
          </motion.button>
        </form>
      </div>

      {attachments.length > 0 && (
        <div className="overflow-hidden bg-[var(--color-bg)] border-t border-[var(--color-border)] chat-fade-slide-in">
          <div className="px-4 py-2.5">
              <div className="max-w-[var(--chat-timeline-max)] mx-auto">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between mb-2">
                  <h4 className="text-xs font-medium text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">
                    {attachments.length} file{attachments.length > 1 ? "s" : ""} selected
                  </h4>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setAttachments([])}
                    className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-danger)] transition-colors"
                  >
                    Remove all
                  </button>
                </div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              {attachments.map((file, index) => (
                <div key={index} className="relative group">
                  {file.type?.startsWith("image/") ? (
                    <div className="relative w-20 h-20 rounded-lg overflow-hidden border border-[var(--color-border)]">
                      <img
                        src={URL.createObjectURL(file)}
                        alt={file.name}
                        className="w-full h-full object-cover"
                      />
                      {file.type === "image/gif" && (
                        <span className="absolute top-1 left-1 bg-black/60 text-white text-[10px] font-bold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">
                          GIF
                        </span>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  ) : file.type?.startsWith("video/") ? (
                    <div className="relative w-20 h-20 rounded-lg overflow-hidden border border-[var(--color-border)] bg-black">
                      <video
                        src={URL.createObjectURL(file)}
                        className="w-full h-full object-cover"
                        muted
                      />
                      <span className="absolute top-1 left-1 bg-black/60 text-white text-[10px] font-bold px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">
                        VID
                      </span>
                    </div>
                  ) : null}
                  <span className="block text-[10px] text-[var(--color-text-muted)] mt-0.5 truncate max-w-20">
                    {file.name}
                  </span>
                  <button
                    type="button"
                    onClick={() => setAttachments((prev) => prev.filter((_, i) => i !== index))}
                    className="absolute -top-1.5 -right-1.5 flex h-5 w-5 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-[var(--color-surface)] border border-[var(--color-border)] shadow-sm text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
                    aria-label={`Remove ${file.name}`}
                  >
                    <X size={10} />
                  </button>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      <ForwardChatModal
        isOpen={Boolean(forwardChat)}
        onClose={() => setForwardChat(null)}
        chat={forwardChat}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

ChatBox.propTypes = {
  conversationHistory: PropTypes.array.isRequired,
  onUpdateConversation: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  onSendMessage: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  currentUserId: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
  onDeleteChat: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  onPinChat: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  onOpenDirectMessage: PropTypes.func,
  userRole: PropTypes.string,
  scrollToMessageId: PropTypes.string,
  selectedThread: PropTypes.string,
  chatRoomId: PropTypes.string,
};

export default ChatBox;
```

FILE: client/services/chat/components/ChatInterface.jsx
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ChatInterface.jsx
import React, { useEffect, useContext } from "react";
import { useGenericSocket } from "@/shared/hooks/useGenericSocket";
import { toast } from "react-toastify";
import ChatBox from "./ChatBox";
import { AuthContext } from "@/shared/context/AuthContext";
import { fetchWithAuth } from "@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth";

const ChatInterface = ({
  chatRoomId,
  selectedThread,
  conversationHistory,
  onUpdateConversation,
  onDeleteFromConversation,
  onSendMessage,
  newThreadTitle,
  setNewThreadTitle,
  currentUserId,
  updateUnreadCounts,
  scrollToMessageId,
  selectedRoomName,
  selectedThreadTitle,
  onOpenDirectMessage,
}) => {
  const { socket } = useGenericSocket("chat");
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (socket && selectedThread) {
      socket.emit("joinThread", selectedThread);

      const handleNewChat = (chat) => {
        if (chat.threadId === selectedThread) {
          onUpdateConversation(chat);
        }
      };

      const handleChatDeleted = ({ chatId, threadId }) => {
        if (threadId === selectedThread && typeof onDeleteFromConversation === "function") {
          onDeleteFromConversation(chatId);
        }
      };

      const handleChatUpdated = (updatedChat) => {
        if (updatedChat.threadId === selectedThread) {
          onUpdateConversation(updatedChat);
        }
      };

      const handleChatRead = ({ chatId, readReceipt }) => {
        onUpdateConversation({
          id: chatId,
          _mergeReadReceipt: readReceipt,
        });
      };

      socket.on("newChat", handleNewChat);
      socket.on("chatDeleted", handleChatDeleted);
      socket.on("chatUpdated", handleChatUpdated);
      socket.on("chatRead", handleChatRead);

      return () => {
        socket.emit("leaveThread", selectedThread);
        socket.off("newChat", handleNewChat);
        socket.off("chatDeleted", handleChatDeleted);
        socket.off("chatUpdated", handleChatUpdated);
        socket.off("chatRead", handleChatRead);
      };
    }
  }, [socket, selectedThread, onUpdateConversation, onDeleteFromConversation]);

  const handleDeleteChat = async (chatId) => {
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chats/${chatId}`,
        { method: "DELETE" }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || "Failed to delete message.");
      }
      if (typeof onDeleteFromConversation === "function") {
        onDeleteFromConversation(chatId);
      }
      toast.success("Message deleted.");
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Delete Chat Error:", error);
      toast.error(`Error: ${error.message}`);
    }
  };

  const handlePinChat = async (chatId, isPinned) => {
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chats/${chatId}/pin`,
        {
          method: "PUT",
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify({ isPinned }),
        }
      );

      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || "Failed to update pin status.");
      }
      toast.success(`Message ${isPinned ? "pinned" : "unpinned"}.`);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Pin Chat Error:", error);
      toast.error(`Error: ${error.message}`);
    }
  };

  const handleSendMessage = async (messageContent, attachments, isImportant) => {
    if (!selectedThread) {
      toast.error("Chat room is still opening.");
      return;
    }

    try {
      const formData = new FormData();
      formData.append("threadId", selectedThread);
      formData.append("chatRoomId", chatRoomId);
      formData.append("content", messageContent);
      formData.append("isImportant", isImportant);

      attachments.forEach((file) => {
        formData.append("attachments", file);
      });

      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/sendChat`,
        {
          method: "POST",
          credentials: "include",
          body: formData,
        }
      );

      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || "Failed to send message.");
      }

      const data = await res.json();
      console.log("Message sent, server response:", data);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Send Message Error:", error);
      toast.error(`Error: ${error.message}`);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col flex-1 min-h-0">
      <ChatBox
        conversationHistory={conversationHistory}
        onUpdateConversation={onUpdateConversation}
        onSendMessage={handleSendMessage}
        currentUserId={currentUserId}
        onDeleteChat={handleDeleteChat}
        onPinChat={handlePinChat}
        onOpenDirectMessage={onOpenDirectMessage}
        userRole={user?.role}
        scrollToMessageId={scrollToMessageId}
        selectedThread={selectedThread}
        chatRoomId={chatRoomId}
        selectedRoomName={selectedRoomName}
        selectedThreadTitle={selectedThreadTitle}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

export default ChatInterface;

```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ChatMessageModal.jsx
import React from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import { X } from 'lucide-react';
import ReactMarkdown from 'react-markdown';
import remarkGfm from 'remark-gfm';

const ChatMessageModal = ({ chat, onClose, onGoToChat }) => {
    if (!chat) return null;

    return (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-60 flex items-center justify-center z-[100] p-4">
            <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-2xl w-full max-w-lg flex flex-col max-h-[calc(100vh-2rem)]">
                <div className="p-4 border-b flex justify-between items-center">
                    <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-gray-800">Message Details</h2>
                    <button onClick={onClose} className="p-1 rounded-full text-gray-500 hover:bg-gray-200 hover:text-gray-800">
                        <X size={24} />
                    </button>
                </div>
                <div className="p-6 overflow-y-auto">
                    <div className="mb-4">
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">From</p>
                        <p className="font-semibold text-gray-900">{chat.sender.username}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="mb-4">
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Location</p>
                        <p className="font-semibold text-gray-900">{chat.chatRoom.name}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="mb-4">
                        <p className="text-sm text-gray-500">Sent</p>
                        <p className="font-semibold text-gray-900">{new Date(chat.updatedAt).toLocaleString()}</p>
                    </div>
                    <div className="mt-4 p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded-md prose prose-sm max-w-none">
                        <ReactMarkdown remarkPlugins={[remarkGfm]}>{chat.content}</ReactMarkdown>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div className="px-6 pb-6 pt-4 flex-shrink-0 border-t border-gray-200 bg-gray-50 rounded-b-lg">
                    <button
                        onClick={(e) => {
                            onGoToChat(e, chat);
                            onClose();
                        }}
                        className="btn btn-primary w-full"
                    >
                        Go to Conversation
                    </button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};

ChatMessageModal.propTypes = {
    chat: PropTypes.shape({
        id: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
        content: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
        updatedAt: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
        sender: PropTypes.shape({
            username: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
        }).isRequired,
        chatRoom: PropTypes.shape({
            id: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
            name: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
        }).isRequired,
        thread: PropTypes.shape({
            id: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
            title: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
        }).isRequired,
    }),
    onClose: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
    onGoToChat: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
};

export default ChatMessageModal;
```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ChatPopupManager.jsx
// client/services/chat/components/ChatPopupManager.js
import React, { useContext, useEffect } from "react";
import { toast } from "react-toastify";
import { useGenericSocket } from "@/shared/hooks/useGenericSocket";
import { useRouter } from "next/router";
import { AuthContext } from "@/shared/context/AuthContext";

const ChatPopupManager = () => {
  const { socket } = useGenericSocket("chat");
  const router = useRouter();
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!socket) return;

    const handleNewChat = (chat) => {
      if (router.pathname === "/chat" || chat.sender.id === user?.id) return;

      const chatRoomId = chat.chatRoom?.id || chat.chatRoomId;
      const threadId = chat.thread?.id || chat.threadId;

      // Dispatch event to open or navigate in global chat window
      const openEvent = new CustomEvent("openGlobalChat", {
        detail: { chatRoomId, threadId },
      });
      window.dispatchEvent(openEvent);

      // Show browser notification if window is not focused
      if (document.hidden || !document.hasFocus()) {
        if (Notification.permission === "granted") {
          const notif = new Notification("New Chat Message", { body: chat.content });
          notif.onclick = () => {
            window.focus();
            const focusEvent = new CustomEvent("openGlobalChat", {
              detail: { chatRoomId, threadId },
            });
            window.dispatchEvent(focusEvent);
          };
        }
      }
    };

    socket.on("newChat", handleNewChat);

    return () => {
      socket.off("newChat", handleNewChat);
    };
  }, [socket, router.pathname, user?.id]);

  return null;
};

export default ChatPopupManager;

```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ChatRoomList.jsx
import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from 'framer-motion';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import { AuthContext } from '@/shared/context/AuthContext';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { Plus, Edit, Trash2, Bell, BellOff, MessageCircle, Users, MoreVertical, AtSign } from 'lucide-react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import Select from 'react-select';

const SUPPORT_USER_ID = 'cm5et7qvf0001yqc7k5j0e9sl';

const ChatRoomList = ({ onSelectRoom, chatRooms, selectedRoom, taggedCount = 0, onShowTaggedMessages }) => {
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [showCreateChatRoomModal, setShowCreateChatRoomModal] = useState(false);
  const [showEditChatRoomModal, setShowEditChatRoomModal] = useState(false);
  const [newChatRoomName, setNewChatRoomName] = useState('');
  const [newChatRoomDescription, setNewChatRoomDescription] = useState('');
  const [isPrivate, setIsPrivate] = useState(false);
  const [shiftNotify, setShiftNotify] = useState(false);
  const [selectedParticipants, setSelectedParticipants] = useState([]);
  const [allUsers, setAllUsers] = useState([]);
  const [chatRoomToEdit, setChatRoomToEdit] = useState(null);
  const [unreadCounts, setUnreadCounts] = useState({});
  const [localChatRooms, setLocalChatRooms] = useState(chatRooms);

  const [menuPortalTarget, setMenuPortalTarget] = useState(null);
  const [openMenuRoomId, setOpenMenuRoomId] = useState(null);
  const menuRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleClickOutside = (e) => {
      if (menuRef.current && !menuRef.current.contains(e.target)) {
        setOpenMenuRoomId(null);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
      setMenuPortalTarget(document.body);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    setLocalChatRooms(chatRooms);
  }, [chatRooms]);

  const canManagePublicRooms =
    user?.role === 'ADMIN' || user?.id === SUPPORT_USER_ID;

  const canEditRooms = canManagePublicRooms;

  const getDisplayRoomName = (room) => {
    if (!room) return '...';
    if (!room.isPrivate) {
      return room.name || 'Untitled Room';
    }
    const participants = Array.isArray(room.participants) ? room.participants : [];
    const otherParticipants = participants.filter(
      (participant) => participant?.id && participant.id !== user?.id
    );
    if (otherParticipants.length === 1) {
      return (
        otherParticipants[0].username ||
        otherParticipants[0].email ||
        room.name ||
        'Direct Message'
      );
    }
    if (otherParticipants.length > 1) {
      const otherNames = otherParticipants
        .map((participant) => participant.username || participant.email)
        .filter(Boolean);
      if (otherNames.length > 0) {
        return otherNames.join(', ');
      }
    }
    return room.name || 'Direct Message';
  };

  const getRoomInitial = (room) => {
    const name = getDisplayRoomName(room);
    return name.charAt(0).toUpperCase();
  };

  const getLastMessagePreview = (room) => {
    const chats = Array.isArray(room.chats) ? room.chats : [];
    if (chats.length === 0) return null;
    const lastChat = chats[chats.length - 1];
    const content = lastChat.content || '';
    const stripped = content.replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '').trim();
    if (!stripped) return 'Sent a message';
    return stripped.length > 60 ? `${stripped.slice(0, 60)}…` : stripped;
  };

  const canDeleteRoom = (room) => {
    if (!room || !user) return false;
    if (canManagePublicRooms) return true;
    if (!room.isPrivate) return false;
    const participants = Array.isArray(room.participants) ? room.participants : [];
    return participants.some((participant) => participant.id === user.id);
  };

  const fetchUnreadCounts = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/unread`,
        { method: 'GET' }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error('Failed to fetch unread counts.');
      }
      const data = await res.json();
      const countsMap = {};
      data.unreadCounts.forEach((item) => {
        countsMap[item.chatRoomId] = item._count.id;
      });
      setUnreadCounts(countsMap);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Fetch Unread Counts Error:', error);
      toast.error('Failed to load unread counts.');
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchUnreadCounts();
  }, [chatRooms]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (showCreateChatRoomModal || showEditChatRoomModal) {
      fetchAllUsers();
    }
  }, [showCreateChatRoomModal, showEditChatRoomModal]);

  const fetchAllUsers = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/user`,
        { method: 'GET' }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        throw new Error('Failed to fetch users.');
      }
      const data = await res.json();
      setAllUsers(data.users);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Fetch Users Error:', error);
      toast.error('Failed to load users for chatroom.');
    }
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    setLoading(false);
  }, [chatRooms]);

  const handleToggleMute = async (e, roomId, currentMuteStatus) => {
    e.stopPropagation();
    setLocalChatRooms((prevRooms) =>
      prevRooms.map((room) =>
        room.id === roomId ? { ...room, isMuted: !currentMuteStatus } : room
      )
    );
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chatrooms/${roomId}/mute`,
        { method: 'PUT' }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Failed to toggle mute status.');
      }
      const data = await res.json();
      toast.success(data.message);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Toggle Mute Error:', error);
      toast.error(`Error: ${error.message}`);
      setLocalChatRooms((prevRooms) =>
        prevRooms.map((room) =>
          room.id === roomId ? { ...room, isMuted: currentMuteStatus } : room
        )
      );
    }
  };

  const handleCreateChatRoom = async () => {
    if (newChatRoomName.trim() === '') {
      toast.error('Chatroom name cannot be empty.');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chatrooms`,
        {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
          body: JSON.stringify({
            name: newChatRoomName,
            description: newChatRoomDescription || null,
            isPrivate,
            shiftNotify: !isPrivate && Boolean(shiftNotify),
            participantIds: isPrivate
              ? selectedParticipants.map((p) => p.value)
              : allUsers.map((listUser) => listUser.id),
          }),
        }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Failed to create chatroom.');
      }
      const data = await res.json();
      toast.success('Chatroom created successfully.');
      onSelectRoom(data.chatRoom.id);
      setNewChatRoomName('');
      setNewChatRoomDescription('');
      setIsPrivate(false);
      setShiftNotify(false);
      setSelectedParticipants([]);
      setShowCreateChatRoomModal(false);
      fetchUnreadCounts();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Create ChatRoom Error:', error);
      toast.error(`Error: ${error.message}`);
    }
  };

  const handleEditChatRoom = (chatRoom) => {
    setChatRoomToEdit(chatRoom);
    setNewChatRoomName(chatRoom.name);
    setNewChatRoomDescription(chatRoom.description || '');
    setIsPrivate(chatRoom.isPrivate);
    setShiftNotify(Boolean(chatRoom.shiftNotify));
    setSelectedParticipants(
      chatRoom.participants.map((participant) => ({
        value: participant.id,
        label: `${participant.username} (${participant.email})`,
      }))
    );
    setShowEditChatRoomModal(true);
  };

  const handleSubmitEditChatRoom = async () => {
    if (newChatRoomName.trim() === '') {
      toast.error('Chatroom name cannot be empty.');
      return;
    }
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chatrooms/${chatRoomToEdit.id}`,
        {
method: 'PUT',
            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
            body: JSON.stringify({
              name: newChatRoomName,
              description: newChatRoomDescription || null,
              isPrivate,
              shiftNotify: !isPrivate && Boolean(shiftNotify),
              participantIds: isPrivate
                ? selectedParticipants.map((p) => p.value)
                : allUsers.map((listUser) => listUser.id),
            }),
        }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Failed to update chatroom.');
      }
      toast.success('Chatroom updated successfully.');
      setShowEditChatRoomModal(false);
      setChatRoomToEdit(null);
      setNewChatRoomName('');
      setIsPrivate(false);
      setShiftNotify(false);
      setSelectedParticipants([]);
      fetchUnreadCounts();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Update ChatRoom Error:', error);
      toast.error(`Error: ${error.message}`);
    }
  };

  const handleDeleteChatRoom = async (room) => {
    if (!canDeleteRoom(room)) {
      toast.error('You do not have permission to delete this chat room.');
      return;
    }
    const roomLabel = getDisplayRoomName(room);
    if (!confirm(`Are you sure you want to delete "${roomLabel}"?`)) return;
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chatrooms/${room.id}`,
        { method: 'DELETE' }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Failed to delete chatroom.');
      }
      setLocalChatRooms((prev) => prev.filter((existingRoom) => existingRoom.id !== room.id));
      toast.success('Chatroom deleted successfully.');
      fetchUnreadCounts();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Delete ChatRoom Error:', error);
      toast.error(`Error: ${error.message}`);
    }
  };

  const handleTogglePrivate = (e) => {
    setIsPrivate(e.target.checked);
    if (!e.target.checked) {
      setSelectedParticipants([]);
    } else {
      setShiftNotify(false);
    }
  };

  const userOptions = allUsers.map((listUser) => ({
    value: listUser.id,
    label: `${listUser.username} (${listUser.email})`,
  }));

  const selectStyles = {
    menuPortal: (base) => ({ ...base, zIndex: 9999 }),
    menu: (base) => ({ ...base, zIndex: 9999 }),
    option: (base, state) => ({
      ...base,
      color: '#0f172a',
      backgroundColor: state.isFocused ? '#f1f5f9' : '#ffffff',
    }),
    singleValue: (base) => ({ ...base, color: '#0f172a' }),
    input: (base) => ({ ...base, color: '#0f172a' }),
    placeholder: (base) => ({ ...base, color: '#94a3b8' }),
  };

  return (
    <div className="flex h-full min-h-0 flex-col">
      <div className="px-4 py-3 border-b border-[var(--color-border)] flex items-center justify-between">
        <button
          onClick={() => setShowCreateChatRoomModal(true)}
          className="flex items-center gap-1.5 bg-[#6b4bd8] text-white text-sm font-medium px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#5438df] transition-colors shadow-sm"
        >
          <Plus size={16} />
          New Chat
        </button>
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={onShowTaggedMessages}
          className={`relative flex h-9 w-9 items-center justify-center rounded-lg border transition-colors ${
            taggedCount > 0
              ? 'border-[#d9ccff] bg-[#f0ebff] text-[#6b4bd8] hover:bg-[#e6ddff]'
              : 'border-[var(--color-border)] text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)]'
          }`}
          aria-label="Show tagged messages"
          title="Tagged messages"
        >
          <AtSign size={16} />
          {taggedCount > 0 && (
            <span className="absolute -right-1 -top-1 flex h-5 min-w-5 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-[#e04498] px-1 text-[10px] font-bold leading-none text-white">
              {taggedCount > 99 ? '99+' : taggedCount}
            </span>
          )}
        </button>
      </div>

      <div className="min-h-0 flex-1 overflow-y-auto py-1">
        {loading ? (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
            className="flex items-center justify-center py-8"
          >
            <span className="loading loading-spinner loading-sm text-[var(--color-text-muted)]" />
          </motion.div>
        ) : localChatRooms.length === 0 ? (
          <motion.div
            initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
            animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
            transition={{ duration: 0.3 }}
            className="px-4 py-8 text-center"
          >
            <MessageCircle size={32} className="mx-auto text-[var(--color-text-muted)] mb-2" />
            <p className="text-sm text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">No chat rooms available.</p>
            <p className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)] mt-1">Create one to get started!</p>
          </motion.div>
        ) : (
          <AnimatePresence mode="popLayout">
            {localChatRooms.map((room, index) => {
            const roomLabel = getDisplayRoomName(room);
            const unread = unreadCounts[room.id] || 0;
            const preview = getLastMessagePreview(room);
            const isActive = selectedRoom === room.id;

            return (
              <motion.div
                key={room.id}
                initial={{ opacity: 0, x: -16 }}
                animate={{ opacity: 1, x: 0 }}
                exit={{ opacity: 0, x: -16 }}
                transition={{ duration: 0.2, delay: index * 0.03, ease: "easeOut" }}
                whileHover={{ x: 3 }}
              >
                <div
                key={room.id}
                className={`chat-room-item group ${isActive ? 'active' : ''}`}
                onClick={() => onSelectRoom(room.id)}
                role="button"
                tabIndex={0}
                onKeyDown={(e) => { if (e.key === 'Enter') onSelectRoom(room.id); }}
              >
                <div className={`chat-room-avatar ${room.isPrivate ? 'private' : 'public'}`}>
                  {getRoomInitial(room)}
                </div>
                <div className="chat-room-info">
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <span className="chat-room-name" title={roomLabel}>{roomLabel}</span>
                    {room.isPrivate && (
                      <span className="chat-room-badge private-pill">DM</span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  {room.description && (
                    <div className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)] truncate mt-0.5" title={room.description}>{room.description}</div>
                  )}
                  <div className="chat-room-preview">
                    {preview}
                  </div>
                </div>
                <div className="chat-room-meta">
                  {unread > 0 && !room.isMuted && (
                    <span className="chat-room-badge unread">
                      {unread > 99 ? '99+' : unread}
                    </span>
                  )}
                  {/* Desktop hover buttons */}
                  <div className="hidden sm:flex items-center gap-0.5 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 pointer-events-none group-hover:pointer-events-auto transition-opacity">
                    <button
                      onClick={(e) => handleToggleMute(e, room.id, room.isMuted)}
                      className="flex h-7 w-7 items-center justify-center rounded-md text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] transition-colors"
                      aria-label={room.isMuted ? `Unmute ${roomLabel}` : `Mute ${roomLabel}`}
                      title={room.isMuted ? `Unmute ${roomLabel}` : `Mute ${roomLabel}`}
                    >
                      {room.isMuted ? <BellOff size={14} /> : <Bell size={14} />}
                    </button>
                    {canEditRooms && (
                      <button
                        onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); handleEditChatRoom(room); }}
                        className="flex h-7 w-7 items-center justify-center rounded-md text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] transition-colors"
                        aria-label={`Edit ${roomLabel}`}
                        title={`Edit ${roomLabel}`}
                      >
                        <Edit size={14} />
                      </button>
                    )}
                    {canDeleteRoom(room) && (
                      <button
                        onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); handleDeleteChatRoom(room); }}
                        className="flex h-7 w-7 items-center justify-center rounded-md text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-danger)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] transition-colors"
                        aria-label={`Delete ${roomLabel}`}
                        title={`Delete ${roomLabel}`}
                      >
                        <Trash2 size={14} />
                      </button>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  {/* Mobile 3-dot menu */}
                  <div className="sm:hidden relative">
                    <button
                      onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); setOpenMenuRoomId(openMenuRoomId === room.id ? null : room.id); }}
                      className="flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-md text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] transition-colors"
                      aria-label="More options"
                    >
                      <MoreVertical size={16} />
                    </button>
                    {openMenuRoomId === room.id && (
                      <div
                        ref={menuRef}
                        className="absolute right-0 top-full mt-1 z-50 w-44 bg-[var(--color-surface)] rounded-xl shadow-lg border border-[var(--color-border)] py-1"
                      >
                        <button
                          onClick={(e) => { handleToggleMute(e, room.id, room.isMuted); setOpenMenuRoomId(null); }}
                          className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm"
                        >
                          {room.isMuted ? <BellOff size={14} /> : <Bell size={14} />}
                          {room.isMuted ? 'Unmute' : 'Mute'}
                        </button>
                        {canEditRooms && (
                          <button
                            onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); handleEditChatRoom(room); setOpenMenuRoomId(null); }}
                            className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm"
                          >
                            <Edit size={14} /> Edit
                          </button>
                        )}
                        {canDeleteRoom(room) && (
                          <button
                            onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); handleDeleteChatRoom(room); setOpenMenuRoomId(null); }}
                            className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-error"
                          >
                            <Trash2 size={14} /> Delete
                          </button>
                        )}
</div>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </motion.div>
            );
          })}
          </AnimatePresence>
        )}
      </div>

      {showCreateChatRoomModal && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
          <div className="bg-[var(--color-surface)] p-6 rounded-xl shadow-xl w-96 max-h-full overflow-y-auto border border-[var(--color-border)]">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-4 text-[var(--color-text-primary)]">Create New Chat Room</h3>
            <div className="mb-4">
              <label className="block mb-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Chatroom Name:</label>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={newChatRoomName}
                onChange={(e) => setNewChatRoomName(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Enter chatroom name..."
                className="w-full border border-[var(--color-border)] rounded-lg px-3 py-2 bg-[var(--color-bg)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[var(--color-brand)]"
              />
            </div>
            <div className="mb-4">
              <label className="block mb-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Description (optional):</label>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={newChatRoomDescription}
                onChange={(e) => setNewChatRoomDescription(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="What is this room about?"
                className="w-full border border-[var(--color-border)] rounded-lg px-3 py-2 bg-[var(--color-bg)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[var(--color-brand)]"
              />
            </div>
            <div className="mb-4">
              <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">
                <input type="checkbox" checked={isPrivate} onChange={handleTogglePrivate} className="rounded" />
                Private Chat
              </label>
            </div>

            {isPrivate && (
              <div className="mb-4">
                <label className="block mb-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Select Participants:</label>
                <Select
                  isMulti
                  options={userOptions}
                  value={selectedParticipants}
                  onChange={setSelectedParticipants}
                  className="react-select-container"
                  classNamePrefix="react-select"
                  placeholder="Select participants..."
                  noOptionsMessage={() => 'No users found'}
                  isSearchable
                  menuPortalTarget={menuPortalTarget}
                  menuPosition="fixed"
                  styles={selectStyles}
                />
              </div>
            )}

            {!isPrivate && (
              <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg border border-[var(--color-border)] bg-[var(--color-bg)] p-3">
                <label className="flex items-start gap-3">
                  <input type="checkbox" checked={shiftNotify} onChange={(e) => setShiftNotify(e.target.checked)} className="mt-1" />
                  <span className="text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">
                    <span className="block font-medium">ShiftChat scheduled notifications</span>
                    <span className="block text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)] mt-0.5">
                      Notify users from 30 minutes before their scheduled shift starts until 30 minutes after it ends.
                    </span>
                  </span>
                </label>
              </div>
            )}

            {!isPrivate && (
              <div className="mb-4">
                <label className="block mb-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Participants:</label>
                <p className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">All users in the organization will be included.</p>
              </div>
            )}

            <div className="flex justify-end gap-2">
              <button
                onClick={() => {
                  setShowCreateChatRoomModal(false);
                  setNewChatRoomName('');
                  setNewChatRoomDescription('');
                  setIsPrivate(false);
                  setShiftNotify(false);
                  setSelectedParticipants([]);
                }}
                className="px-4 py-2 bg-[var(--color-bg)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] rounded-lg hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] text-sm transition-colors"
              >
                Cancel
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={handleCreateChatRoom}
                className="px-4 py-2 bg-[#6b4bd8] text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-[#5438df] text-sm transition-colors"
              >
                Create
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {showEditChatRoomModal && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/50 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
          <div className="bg-[var(--color-surface)] p-6 rounded-xl shadow-xl w-96 max-h-full overflow-y-auto border border-[var(--color-border)]">
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold mb-4 text-[var(--color-text-primary)]">Edit Chat Room</h3>
            <div className="mb-4">
              <label className="block mb-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Chatroom Name:</label>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={newChatRoomName}
                onChange={(e) => setNewChatRoomName(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Enter chatroom name..."
                className="w-full border border-[var(--color-border)] rounded-lg px-3 py-2 bg-[var(--color-bg)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[var(--color-brand)]"
              />
            </div>
            <div className="mb-4">
              <label className="block mb-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Description (optional):</label>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={newChatRoomDescription}
                onChange={(e) => setNewChatRoomDescription(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="What is this room about?"
                className="w-full border border-[var(--color-border)] rounded-lg px-3 py-2 bg-[var(--color-bg)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-[var(--color-brand)]"
              />
            </div>
            <div className="mb-4">
              <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">
                <input type="checkbox" checked={isPrivate} onChange={handleTogglePrivate} className="rounded" />
                Private Chat
              </label>
            </div>

            {isPrivate && (
              <div className="mb-4">
                <label className="block mb-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Select Participants:</label>
                <Select
                  isMulti
                  options={userOptions}
                  value={selectedParticipants}
                  onChange={setSelectedParticipants}
                  className="react-select-container"
                  classNamePrefix="react-select"
                  placeholder="Select participants..."
                  noOptionsMessage={() => 'No users found'}
                  isSearchable
                  menuPortalTarget={menuPortalTarget}
                  menuPosition="fixed"
                  styles={selectStyles}
                />
              </div>
            )}

            {!isPrivate && (
              <div className="mb-4 rounded-lg border border-[var(--color-border)] bg-[var(--color-bg)] p-3">
                <label className="flex items-start gap-3">
                  <input type="checkbox" checked={shiftNotify} onChange={(e) => setShiftNotify(e.target.checked)} className="mt-1" />
                  <span className="text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">
                    <span className="block font-medium">ShiftChat scheduled notifications</span>
                    <span className="block text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)] mt-0.5">
                      Notify users from 30 minutes before their scheduled shift starts until 30 minutes after it ends.
                    </span>
                  </span>
                </label>
              </div>
            )}

            {!isPrivate && (
              <div className="mb-4">
                <label className="block mb-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Participants:</label>
                <p className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">All users in the organization will be included.</p>
              </div>
            )}

            <div className="flex justify-end gap-2">
              <button
                onClick={() => {
                  setShowEditChatRoomModal(false);
                  setChatRoomToEdit(null);
                  setNewChatRoomName('');
                  setNewChatRoomDescription('');
                  setIsPrivate(false);
                  setShiftNotify(false);
                  setSelectedParticipants([]);
                }}
                className="px-4 py-2 bg-[var(--color-bg)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] rounded-lg hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] text-sm transition-colors"
              >
                Cancel
              </button>
              <button
                onClick={handleSubmitEditChatRoom}
                className="px-4 py-2 bg-[#6b4bd8] text-white rounded-lg hover:bg-[#5438df] text-sm transition-colors"
              >
                Update
              </button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

ChatRoomList.propTypes = {
  onSelectRoom: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  chatRooms: PropTypes.array.isRequired,
  selectedRoom: PropTypes.string,
  taggedCount: PropTypes.number,
  onShowTaggedMessages: PropTypes.func,
};

export default ChatRoomList;

```
