FILE: client/services/chat/components/ChatRoomSettingsModal.jsx
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ChatRoomSettingsModal.jsx
import React, { useContext, useEffect, useMemo, useState } from "react";
import PropTypes from "prop-types";
import { toast } from "react-toastify";
import { fetchWithAuth } from "@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth";
import { AuthContext } from "@/shared/context/AuthContext";
import { Settings2, Save, Bell, BellOff } from "lucide-react";

const SUPPORT_USER_ID = "cm5et7qvf0001yqc7k5j0e9sl";

const ChatRoomSettingsModal = ({ isOpen, onClose, room, onRoomUpdated }) => {
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);

  const [roomName, setRoomName] = useState("");
  const [roomDescription, setRoomDescription] = useState("");
  const [shiftNotify, setShiftNotify] = useState(false);
  const [isMuted, setIsMuted] = useState(false);
  const [saving, setSaving] = useState(false);
  const [togglingMute, setTogglingMute] = useState(false);

  const canManageRoom =
    user?.role === "ADMIN" || user?.id === SUPPORT_USER_ID;

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!isOpen || !room) return;
    setRoomName(room.name || "");
    setRoomDescription(room.description || "");
    setShiftNotify(Boolean(room.shiftNotify));
    setIsMuted(Boolean(room.isMuted));
  }, [isOpen, room]);

  const roomLabel = useMemo(() => {
    if (!room) return "";
    return room.displayName || room.name || "Chat Room";
  }, [room]);

  if (!isOpen || !room) return null;

  const handleSave = async () => {
    if (!canManageRoom) return;

    if (!roomName.trim() && !room.isPrivate) {
      toast.error("Chatroom name cannot be empty.");
      return;
    }

    try {
      setSaving(true);

      const payload = {
        name: room.isPrivate ? room.name : roomName.trim(),
        description: roomDescription || null,
        shiftNotify: Boolean(shiftNotify),
      };

      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chatrooms/${room.id}`,
        {
          method: "PUT",
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
          body: JSON.stringify(payload),
        }
      );

      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
        throw new Error(errorData.error || "Failed to update chatroom.");
      }

      const data = await res.json();
      const updatedRoom = {
        ...room,
        ...data.chatRoom,
        isMuted,
        displayName: room.displayName,
      };

      onRoomUpdated?.(updatedRoom);
      toast.success("Chatroom settings updated.");
      onClose();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Update ChatRoom Settings Error:", error);
      toast.error(error.message || "Failed to update chatroom.");
    } finally {
      setSaving(false);
    }
  };

  const handleToggleMute = async () => {
    try {
      setTogglingMute(true);

      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chatrooms/${room.id}/mute`,
        { method: "PUT" }
      );

      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json().catch(() => ({}));
        throw new Error(errorData.error || "Failed to toggle mute status.");
      }

      const data = await res.json();
      const nextMuted = Boolean(data.isMuted);

      setIsMuted(nextMuted);
      onRoomUpdated?.({
        ...room,
        isMuted: nextMuted,
        displayName: room.displayName,
      });

      toast.success(data.message || "Chatroom mute updated.");
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Toggle Mute Error:", error);
      toast.error(error.message || "Failed to toggle mute status.");
    } finally {
      setTogglingMute(false);
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className={`modal ${isOpen ? "modal-open" : ""}`}>
      <div className="modal-box max-w-lg relative">
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={onClose}
          className="btn btn-sm btn-circle btn-ghost absolute right-3 top-3"
          title="Close"
        >
          ✕
        </button>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-5">
          <div className="rounded-full bg-primary/10 text-primary p-2">
            <Settings2 size={18} />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="font-bold text-xl">Chatroom Settings</h3>
            <p className="text-sm text-base-content/70 truncate">
              {roomLabel}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="space-y-5">
          {!room.isPrivate && (
            <div className="form-control">
              <label className="label" htmlFor="chatroom-name">
                <span className="label-text font-semibold">Name</span>
              </label>
              <input
                id="chatroom-name"
                type="text"
                value={roomName}
                onChange={(e) => setRoomName(e.target.value)}
                className="input input-bordered w-full"
                disabled={!canManageRoom || saving}
                placeholder="Chatroom name"
              />
            </div>
          )}

          {!room.isPrivate && (
            <div className="form-control">
              <label className="label" htmlFor="chatroom-description">
                <span className="label-text font-semibold">Description (optional)</span>
              </label>
              <input
                id="chatroom-description"
                type="text"
                value={roomDescription}
                onChange={(e) => setRoomDescription(e.target.value)}
                className="input input-bordered w-full"
                disabled={!canManageRoom || saving}
                placeholder="What is this room about?"
              />
            </div>
          )}

          {room.isPrivate && (
            <div className="alert">
              <span className="text-sm">
                Direct message titles are shown from the other participant’s name.
              </span>
            </div>
          )}

          <div className="form-control">
            <label className="label cursor-pointer justify-start gap-3">
              <input
                type="checkbox"
                className="toggle toggle-primary"
                checked={shiftNotify}
                onChange={(e) => setShiftNotify(e.target.checked)}
                disabled={!canManageRoom || room.isPrivate || saving}
              />
              <div>
                <div className="font-medium">ShiftChat scheduled notifications</div>
                <div className="text-xs text-base-content/70">
                  Automatically notify users from 30 minutes before their scheduled shift starts until 30 minutes after it ends.
                </div>
              </div>
            </label>
          </div>

          <div className="pt-2 border-t border-base-300 flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
            <div>
              <div className="font-medium">
                {isMuted ? "Muted" : "Notifications on"}
              </div>
              <div className="text-xs text-base-content/70">
                Mute or unmute this room for your account.
              </div>
            </div>
            <button
              type="button"
              className={`btn ${isMuted ? "btn-outline" : "btn-primary"}`}
              onClick={handleToggleMute}
              disabled={togglingMute}
            >
              {isMuted ? <BellOff size={16} /> : <Bell size={16} />}
              {togglingMute
                ? "Updating..."
                : isMuted
                ? "Unmute"
                : "Mute"}
            </button>
          </div>

          {!canManageRoom && (
            <div className="text-xs text-base-content/60">
              Rename and ShiftChat settings require admin access. Mute/unmute is always available.
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        <div className="modal-action">
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={onClose}
            className="btn btn-ghost"
            disabled={saving}
          >
            Cancel
          </button>

          {canManageRoom && (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={handleSave}
              className={`btn btn-primary ${saving ? "loading" : ""}`}
              disabled={saving}
            >
              {!saving && <Save size={16} />}
              Save
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      <form method="dialog" className="modal-backdrop">
        <button onClick={onClose}>close</button>
      </form>
    </div>
  );
};

ChatRoomSettingsModal.propTypes = {
  isOpen: PropTypes.bool.isRequired,
  onClose: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  room: PropTypes.object,
  onRoomUpdated: PropTypes.func,
};

export default ChatRoomSettingsModal;
```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ChatWidget.jsx
import React, { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { MessageSquare, Pin, Bell, X } from 'lucide-react';
import BaseWidget from '@/shared/components/BaseWidget';
import ChatMessageModal from './ChatMessageModal';
import { useRouter } from 'next/router';
import ReactMarkdown from 'react-markdown';
import remarkGfm from 'remark-gfm';

const ChatWidget = () => {
    const [widgetData, setWidgetData] = useState({
        pinnedChats: [],
        importantChats: [],
        recentChats: [],
    });
    const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
    const [selectedChat, setSelectedChat] = useState(null);
    const router = useRouter();

    const fetchWidgetData = useCallback(async () => {
        setLoading(true);
        try {
            const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/widget`);
            if (res.ok) {
                const data = await res.json();
                setWidgetData(data);
            } else {
                toast.error("Failed to load chat data.");
            }
        } catch (error) {
            console.error("Fetch Chat Widget Data Error:", error);
            toast.error("An error occurred while fetching chat data.");
        } finally {
            setLoading(false);
        }
    }, []);

    useEffect(() => {
        fetchWidgetData();
    }, [fetchWidgetData]);

    const handleMessageClick = (chat) => {
        setSelectedChat(chat);
    };

    const handleAction = async (e, chat, type) => {
        e.stopPropagation();

        if (type === 'pinned') {
            const url = `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/widget/${chat.id}/dismiss`;
            try {
                const res = await fetchWithAuth(url, { method: 'PUT' });
                if (!res.ok) {
                    const errorData = await res.json();
                    throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Failed to dismiss pinned message');
                }
                toast.success('Pinned message dismissed.');
                fetchWidgetData();
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Dismiss pinned message error:', error);
                toast.error(error.message);
            }
        } else if (type === 'important') {
            const url = `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/widget/${chat.id}/dismiss`;
            try {
                const res = await fetchWithAuth(url, { method: 'PUT' });
                if (!res.ok) {
                    const errorData = await res.json();
                    throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Failed to dismiss message');
                }
                toast.success('Message dismissed.');
                fetchWidgetData();
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('Dismiss error:', error);
                toast.error(error.message);
            }
        }
    };
    
    const goToChat = (e, chat) => {
        e.stopPropagation();
        router.push(`/chat?chatRoomId=${chat.chatRoom.id}&threadId=${chat.thread.id}`);
    };

    const renderChatItem = (chat, type) => (
        <li
            key={chat.id}
            className="p-2 rounded-md hover:bg-gray-100 dark:hover:bg-gray-700 cursor-pointer flex justify-between items-center group"
            onClick={() => handleMessageClick(chat)}
        >
            <div className="flex-1 overflow-hidden">
                <div className="flex items-center space-x-2">
                    <span className="text-sm font-semibold truncate">{chat.sender.username}</span>
                    <span className="text-xs text-gray-500 dark:text-gray-400 whitespace-nowrap">{new Date(chat.updatedAt).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })}</span>
                </div>
                <div className="text-sm text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-500 line-clamp-3 [&>p]:m-0">
                  <ReactMarkdown remarkPlugins={[remarkGfm]}>{chat.content}</ReactMarkdown>
                </div>
                 <p className="text-xs text-gray-400 dark:text-gray-300 truncate">
                    {chat.chatRoom.name}
                </p>
            </div>
            {(type === 'pinned' || type === 'important') && (
                <button
                    onClick={(e) => handleAction(e, chat, type)}
                    className="ml-2 p-1 text-gray-400 hover:text-gray-600 rounded-full opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
                    title={type === 'pinned' ? 'Unpin' : 'Dismiss'}
                >
                    <X size={16} />
                </button>
            )}
        </li>
    );

    const renderSection = (title, icon, chats, type) => {
        if (!chats || chats.length === 0) return null;
        return (
            <div className="border-b border-gray-200 dark:border-gray-700 last:border-b-0 pb-3 last:pb-0">
                <h3 className="text-md font-semibold text-gray-700 dark:text-gray-300 flex items-center mb-1 px-2">
                    {icon}
                    <span className="ml-2">{title}</span>
                </h3>
                <ul className="space-y-1">
                    {chats.map(chat => renderChatItem(chat, type))}
                </ul>
            </div>
        );
    };

    return (
        <>
            <BaseWidget title="Chat" path="/chat" icon={<MessageSquare />}>
                <div className="p-2 space-y-3">
                    {loading ? (
                        <div className="text-center p-4">Loading...</div>
                    ) : (
                        <>
                            {renderSection('Pinned Messages', <Pin size={16} className="text-yellow-500" />, widgetData.pinnedChats, 'pinned')}
                            {renderSection('Important Messages', <Bell size={16} className="text-red-500" />, widgetData.importantChats, 'important')}
                            {renderSection('Recent Messages', <MessageSquare size={16} className="text-blue-500" />, widgetData.recentChats, 'recent')}
                            
                            {widgetData.pinnedChats.length === 0 && widgetData.importantChats.length === 0 && widgetData.recentChats.length === 0 && (
                                <p className="text-center text-gray-500 p-4">No new activity.</p>
                            )}
                        </>
                    )}
                </div>
            </BaseWidget>
            {selectedChat && (
                <ChatMessageModal
                    chat={selectedChat}
                    onClose={() => setSelectedChat(null)}
                    onGoToChat={goToChat}
                />
            )}
        </>
    );
};

export default ChatWidget;

```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ConversationList.jsx
import React, { useContext, useEffect, useLayoutEffect, useRef, useState, useMemo, useCallback } from "react";
import PropTypes from "prop-types";
import { motion, AnimatePresence } from "framer-motion";

const bubbleVariants = {
  initial: { opacity: 0, scale: 0.85, y: 12 },
  animate: { opacity: 1, scale: 1, y: 0 },
  exit: { opacity: 0, scale: 0.85, y: -8 },
};

const groupVariants = {
  initial: {},
  animate: {
    transition: { staggerChildren: 0.04 },
  },
};
import ReactMarkdown from "react-markdown";
import remarkGfm from "remark-gfm";
import {
  MoreVertical,
  Star,
  Trash2,
  Pin,
  CheckCheck,
  Reply,
  Forward,
  Link2,
  MessageSquare,
  AtSign,
  Info,
  Phone,
  ChevronDown,
  X,
  List,
} from "lucide-react";

import CreateNoteModal from "@/services/notes/components/CreateNoteModal";
import CreateTaskModal from "@/services/tasks/components/CreateTaskModal";
import CallsService from "@/services/calls/CallsService";
import { AuthContext } from "@/shared/context/AuthContext";
import { fetchWithAuth } from "@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth";
import { getActionSuggestions } from "@/services/chat/utils/actionSuggestions";
import ActionSuggestionBar from "@/services/chat/components/ActionSuggestionBar";
import ReactionsDisplay from "@/services/chat/components/ReactionsDisplay";

const GROUP_TIME_WINDOW = 5 * 60 * 1000;
const useIsomorphicLayoutEffect =
  typeof window === "undefined" ? useEffect : useLayoutEffect;

const isSafeLink = (href = "") => /^(https?:\/\/|mailto:|\/)/i.test(String(href).trim());

const stripHtmlTags = (value = "") =>
  String(value)
    .replace(/<br\s*\/?>/gi, "\n")
    .replace(/<[^>]*>/g, "")
    .trim();

const escapeHtml = (value = "") =>
  String(value)
    .replace(/&/g, "&amp;")
    .replace(/</g, "&lt;")
    .replace(/>/g, "&gt;")
    .replace(/"/g, "&quot;")
    .replace(/'/g, "&#39;");

const isInternalAppLink = (href = "") => {
  if (!href) return false;
  if (href.startsWith("/")) return true;
  if (typeof window === "undefined") return false;
  try {
    const url = new URL(href, window.location.origin);
    return url.origin === window.location.origin;
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
};

const renderPlainText = (text, keyPrefix) => {
  const parts = String(text).split("\n");
  return parts.map((part, index) => (
    <React.Fragment key={`${keyPrefix}-${index}`}>
      {part}
      {index < parts.length - 1 ? <br /> : null}
    </React.Fragment>
  ));
};

const renderMentions = (text, keyPrefix) => {
  const nodes = [];
  const mentionPattern = /@([A-Za-z0-9_][A-Za-z0-9_.-]{0,31})\b/g;
  let lastIndex = 0;
  let match;
  while ((match = mentionPattern.exec(String(text))) !== null) {
    if (match.index > lastIndex) {
      nodes.push(...renderPlainText(String(text).slice(lastIndex, match.index), `${keyPrefix}-text-${lastIndex}`));
    }
    nodes.push(
      <span
        key={`${keyPrefix}-mention-${match.index}`}
        className="rounded bg-[var(--color-brand-light)] px-1 font-semibold text-[var(--color-brand)]"
      >
        @{match[1]}
      </span>
    );
    lastIndex = match.index + match[0].length;
  }
  if (lastIndex < String(text).length) {
    nodes.push(...renderPlainText(String(text).slice(lastIndex), `${keyPrefix}-tail-${lastIndex}`));
  }
  return nodes.length > 0 ? nodes : renderPlainText(text, keyPrefix);
};

const hasHtmlMarkup = (content = "") => /<\/?[a-z][\s\S]*>/i.test(String(content));

const renderHtmlNodeList = (nodes, keyPrefix) =>
  Array.from(nodes || []).flatMap((node, index) =>
    renderHtmlNode(node, `${keyPrefix}-${index}`)
  );

const renderHtmlNode = (node, key) => {
  if (!node) return null;
  if (node.nodeType === 3) {
    return renderPlainText(node.textContent || "", key);
  }
  if (node.nodeType !== 1) return null;
  const tag = node.tagName.toLowerCase();
  const children = renderHtmlNodeList(node.childNodes, `${key}-child`);
  if (tag === "br") return <br key={key} />;
  if (tag === "strong" || tag === "b") return <strong key={key}>{children}</strong>;
  if (tag === "em" || tag === "i") return <em key={key}>{children}</em>;
  if (tag === "p") return <p key={key} className="mb-1 last:mb-0 whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">{children}</p>;
  if (tag === "blockquote") return <blockquote key={key} className="mt-1 rounded-r-md border-l-4 border-[var(--color-border)] bg-[var(--color-bg)] px-2 py-1 whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">{children}</blockquote>;
  if (tag === "hr") return <hr key={key} className="my-1 border-[var(--color-border)]" />;
  if (tag === "a") {
    const href = String(node.getAttribute("href") || "").trim();
    const label = stripHtmlTags(node.textContent || href);
    const internalLink = isInternalAppLink(href);
    if (!isSafeLink(href)) return renderPlainText(node.textContent || "", key);
    return (
      <a key={key} href={href} target={internalLink ? undefined : "_blank"} rel={internalLink ? undefined : "noopener noreferrer"} className="underline break-all text-[var(--color-brand)] hover:text-[var(--color-brand-hover)] transition-colors">
        {label || href}
      </a>
    );
  }
  if (tag === "div") {
    const contextType = String(node.getAttribute("data-chat-context") || "").trim();
    if (contextType) {
      return <div key={key} className="mt-1 rounded-lg border border-[var(--color-border)] bg-[var(--color-bg)] px-2 py-1">{children}</div>;
    }
    return <div key={key} className="whitespace-pre-wrap break-words">{children}</div>;
  }
  return children;
};

const renderHtmlContent = (content) => {
  if (typeof window === "undefined" || typeof DOMParser === "undefined") {
    return renderPlainText(stripHtmlTags(content), "html-ssr");
  }
  const parser = new DOMParser();
  const doc = parser.parseFromString(String(content), "text/html");
  return renderHtmlNodeList(doc.body.childNodes, "html");
};

const renderTextWithLinks = (content) => {
  const pattern = /<a\s+[^>]*href=(["'])(.*?)\1[^>]*>(.*?)<\/a>|\[([^\]]+)\]\(([^)\s]+)\)/gis;
  const nodes = [];
  let lastIndex = 0;
  let match;
  while ((match = pattern.exec(content)) !== null) {
    const fullMatch = match[0];
    const htmlHref = match[2];
    const htmlLabel = match[3];
    const markdownLabel = match[4];
    const markdownHref = match[5];
    const startIndex = match.index;
    if (startIndex > lastIndex) {
      nodes.push(...renderMentions(content.slice(lastIndex, startIndex), `text-${lastIndex}`));
    }
    const href = (htmlHref || markdownHref || "").trim();
    const label = stripHtmlTags(htmlLabel || markdownLabel || href);
    const internalLink = isInternalAppLink(href);
    if (isSafeLink(href)) {
      nodes.push(
        <a key={`link-${startIndex}`} href={href} target={internalLink ? undefined : "_blank"} rel={internalLink ? undefined : "noopener noreferrer"} className="underline break-all text-[var(--color-brand)] hover:text-[var(--color-brand-hover)] transition-colors">
          {label || href}
        </a>
      );
    } else {
      nodes.push(...renderPlainText(fullMatch, `unsafe-${startIndex}`));
    }
    lastIndex = startIndex + fullMatch.length;
  }
  if (lastIndex < content.length) {
    nodes.push(...renderMentions(content.slice(lastIndex), `tail-${lastIndex}`));
  }
  if (nodes.length === 0) return renderMentions(content, "plain");
  return nodes;
};

const preprocessMentions = (text) =>
  String(text).replace(/@([A-Za-z0-9_][A-Za-z0-9_.-]{0,31})\b/g, "`@$1`");

const renderMarkdownContent = (content) => {
  const processed = preprocessMentions(content);
  return (
    <ReactMarkdown
      remarkPlugins={[remarkGfm]}
      components={{
        p: ({ children }) => <>{children}</>,
        a: ({ href, children }) => {
          if (!isSafeLink(href)) return <>{children}</>;
          const internal = isInternalAppLink(href);
          return (
            <a
              href={href}
              target={internal ? undefined : "_blank"}
              rel={internal ? undefined : "noopener noreferrer"}
              className="underline break-all text-[var(--color-brand)] hover:text-[var(--color-brand-hover)] transition-colors"
            >
              {children}
            </a>
          );
        },
        code: ({ children }) => {
          const text = String(children);
          if (text.startsWith("@")) {
            return (
              <span className="rounded bg-[var(--color-brand-light)] px-1 font-semibold text-[var(--color-brand)]">
                {text}
              </span>
            );
          }
          return (
            <code className="rounded bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] px-1 py-0.5 text-sm">
              {children}
            </code>
          );
        },
      }}
    >
      {processed}
    </ReactMarkdown>
  );
};

const renderChatContent = (content) => {
  if (!content || typeof content !== "string") return null;
  if (hasHtmlMarkup(content)) return renderHtmlContent(content);
  return renderMarkdownContent(content);
};

const buildChatUrl = (chat) => {
  const chatRoomId = chat?.chatRoomId || chat?.chatRoom?.id || chat?.thread?.chatRoomId;
  const threadId = chat?.threadId || chat?.thread?.id;
  const messageId = chat?.id;
  if (!chatRoomId || !threadId || !messageId) return "";
  if (typeof window === "undefined") {
    return `/chat?chatRoomId=${encodeURIComponent(chatRoomId)}&threadId=${encodeURIComponent(threadId)}&messageId=${encodeURIComponent(messageId)}`;
  }
  const url = new URL("/chat", window.location.origin);
  url.searchParams.set("chatRoomId", chatRoomId);
  url.searchParams.set("threadId", threadId);
  url.searchParams.set("messageId", messageId);
  return url.toString();
};

const buildChatSnippet = (chat) => {
  const content = stripHtmlTags(chat?.contentHtml || chat?.content || "");
  if (!content) return "Message";
  return content.length > 120 ? `${content.slice(0, 120)}…` : content;
};

const buildTaskTitle = (chat) => {
  const snippet = buildChatSnippet(chat);
  return `Follow up: ${snippet}`;
};

const buildNoteTitle = (chat) => {
  const sender = chat?.sender?.username || "Chat";
  const snippet = buildChatSnippet(chat);
  return `${sender}: ${snippet}`;
};

const buildQuotedHtml = (chat) => {
  const sender = chat?.sender?.username || "Unknown";
  const room = chat?.chatRoom?.name || "Unknown room";
  const sentAt = chat?.updatedAt || chat?.createdAt;
  const chatUrl = buildChatUrl(chat);
  const body = escapeHtml(stripHtmlTags(chat?.contentHtml || chat?.content || "")).replace(/\n/g, "<br />");
  return `
    <p><strong>Sender:</strong> ${escapeHtml(sender)}</p>
    <p><strong>Chat Room:</strong> ${escapeHtml(room)}</p>
    ${sentAt ? `<p><strong>Sent:</strong> ${escapeHtml(new Date(sentAt).toLocaleString())}</p>` : ""}
    ${chatUrl ? `<p><strong>Link:</strong> <a href="${escapeHtml(chatUrl)}" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Open original chat</a></p>` : ""}
    <hr />
    <p>${body}</p>
  `.trim();
};

const formatDateLabel = (isoString) => {
  if (!isoString) return null;
  const date = new Date(isoString);
  if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return null;
  const today = new Date();
  const yesterday = new Date(today);
  yesterday.setDate(yesterday.getDate() - 1);
  if (date.toDateString() === today.toDateString()) return "Today";
  if (date.toDateString() === yesterday.toDateString()) return "Yesterday";
  return date.toLocaleDateString("en-US", { month: "long", day: "numeric", year: "numeric" });
};

const formatTime = (isoString) => {
  if (!isoString) return "";
  const date = new Date(isoString);
  if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return "";
  return date.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: "2-digit", minute: "2-digit" });
};

const ConversationList = ({
  conversationHistory,
  currentUserId,
  userRole,
  markAsRead,
  confirmRead,
  onDeleteChat,
  onPinChat,
  onReplyToChat,
  onForwardChat,
  onOpenDirectMessage,
  scrollToMessageId,
  scrollToMessageRequestToken,
  selectedThread,
}) => {
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);
  const timelineRef = useRef(null);
  const messagesEndRef = useRef(null);
  const messageRefs = useRef({});
  const hasScrolledToId = useRef(false);
  const scrollPositionRef = useRef({ threadId: null, latestMessageId: null });
  const [openOptionsId, setOpenOptionsId] = useState(null);
  const [showNoteModal, setShowNoteModal] = useState(false);
  const [showTaskModal, setShowTaskModal] = useState(false);
  const [selectedChat, setSelectedChat] = useState(null);
  const [orgPhoneNumber, setOrgPhoneNumber] = useState("");
  const [infoChat, setInfoChat] = useState(null);
  const [optionsSide, setOptionsSide] = useState("right");
  const [optionsVertical, setOptionsVertical] = useState("down");
  const [lightboxImg, setLightboxImg] = useState(null);
  const [showJumpLatest, setShowJumpLatest] = useState(false);
  const [isAutoScrolling, setIsAutoScrolling] = useState(true);
  const [dismissedSuggestions, setDismissedSuggestions] = useState(() => new Set());
  const [suggestionAction, setSuggestionAction] = useState(null);
  const [reactionsMap, setReactionsMap] = useState({});
  const [reactionsLoadAttempted, setReactionsLoadAttempted] = useState(false);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!user?.organizationId) return;
    fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/organization/${user.organizationId}`)
      .then((res) => res.ok ? res.json() : null)
      .then((data) => { if (data?.organization?.phoneNumber) setOrgPhoneNumber(data.organization.phoneNumber); })
      .catch(() => {});
  }, [user?.organizationId]);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleClickOutside = (e) => {
      if (openOptionsId) {
        const target = e.target;
        if (!target.closest('.chat-options-menu') && !target.closest('.chat-options-btn')) {
          setOpenOptionsId(null);
        }
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener('mousedown', handleClickOutside);
  }, [openOptionsId]);

  useEffect(() => {
    hasScrolledToId.current = false;
  }, [scrollToMessageId, scrollToMessageRequestToken]);

  useIsomorphicLayoutEffect(() => {
    const latestMessageId = conversationHistory[conversationHistory.length - 1]?.id || null;
    const previousPosition = scrollPositionRef.current;
    const isInitialThreadPosition =
      previousPosition.threadId !== selectedThread ||
      (latestMessageId && !previousPosition.latestMessageId);

    if (scrollToMessageId && messageRefs.current[scrollToMessageId] && !hasScrolledToId.current) {
      const element = messageRefs.current[scrollToMessageId];
      element.scrollIntoView({
        behavior: isInitialThreadPosition ? "auto" : "smooth",
        block: "center",
      });
      element.classList.add("ring-2", "ring-primary", "ring-offset-2", "ring-offset-base-100");
      window.setTimeout(() => {
        element.classList.remove("ring-2", "ring-primary", "ring-offset-2", "ring-offset-base-100");
      }, 1800);
      hasScrolledToId.current = true;
    } else if (isAutoScrolling && messagesEndRef.current) {
      messagesEndRef.current.scrollIntoView({
        behavior: isInitialThreadPosition ? "auto" : "smooth",
        block: "end",
      });
      if (isInitialThreadPosition) {
        setShowJumpLatest(false);
        setIsAutoScrolling(true);
      }
    }

    scrollPositionRef.current = {
      threadId: selectedThread,
      latestMessageId,
    };
  }, [conversationHistory, scrollToMessageId, scrollToMessageRequestToken, isAutoScrolling, selectedThread]);

  const handleScroll = useCallback(() => {
    if (!timelineRef.current) return;
    const { scrollTop, scrollHeight, clientHeight } = timelineRef.current;
    const isNearBottom = scrollHeight - scrollTop - clientHeight < 150;
    setShowJumpLatest(!isNearBottom);
    setIsAutoScrolling(isNearBottom);
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    const el = timelineRef.current;
    if (!el) return;
    el.addEventListener("scroll", handleScroll, { passive: true });
    return () => el.removeEventListener("scroll", handleScroll);
  }, [handleScroll]);

  const scrollToLatest = () => {
    setIsAutoScrolling(true);
    setShowJumpLatest(false);
    if (messagesEndRef.current) {
      messagesEndRef.current.scrollIntoView({ behavior: "smooth" });
    }
  };

  const fetchReactionsForChats = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!Array.isArray(conversationHistory) || conversationHistory.length === 0) return;

    const chatIds = conversationHistory.map((c) => c.id).filter(Boolean);
    if (chatIds.length === 0) return;

    const results = {};
    let hasNewData = false;

    const batchSize = 5;
    for (let i = 0; i < chatIds.length; i += batchSize) {
      const batch = chatIds.slice(i, i + batchSize);
      const promises = batch.map(async (chatId) => {
        try {
          const res = await fetchWithAuth(
            `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/reactions/${chatId}`
          );
          if (res.ok) {
            const data = await res.json();
            return { chatId, reactions: Array.isArray(data.reactions) ? data.reactions : [] };
          }
        } catch {}
        return { chatId, reactions: [] };
      });

      const settled = await Promise.allSettled(promises);
      for (const result of settled) {
        if (result.status === "fulfilled" && result.value) {
          const { chatId, reactions } = result.value;
          const existingKey = JSON.stringify(results[chatId] || []);
          const newKey = JSON.stringify(reactions);
          if (existingKey !== newKey) {
            results[chatId] = reactions;
            hasNewData = true;
          }
        }
      }
    }

    if (hasNewData) {
      setReactionsMap((current) => ({ ...current, ...results }));
    }
    setReactionsLoadAttempted(true);
  }, [conversationHistory]);

  const handleReactionChange = useCallback((change) => {
    if (!change?.chatId) return;

    setReactionsMap((current) => {
      const currentReactions = current[change.chatId] || [];

      if (change.type === "add" && change.reaction) {
        const nextReactions = currentReactions.some((reaction) => reaction.id === change.reaction.id)
          ? currentReactions
          : [...currentReactions, change.reaction];

        return { ...current, [change.chatId]: nextReactions };
      }

      if (change.type === "remove") {
        const nextReactions = currentReactions.filter(
          (reaction) =>
            !(
              reaction.emoji === change.emoji &&
              (reaction.user?.id === change.userId || reaction.userId === change.userId)
            )
        );

        return { ...current, [change.chatId]: nextReactions };
      }

      return current;
    });
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!reactionsLoadAttempted && conversationHistory.length > 0) {
      fetchReactionsForChats();
    }
  }, [conversationHistory, reactionsLoadAttempted, fetchReactionsForChats]);

  // Group messages by sender within time window
  const groupedMessages = useMemo(() => {
    if (!Array.isArray(conversationHistory) || conversationHistory.length === 0) return [];
    const groups = [];
    let currentGroup = null;
    conversationHistory.forEach((chat) => {
      const isCurrentUser = chat.sender?.id === currentUserId;
      const chatTime = new Date(chat.updatedAt || chat.createdAt).getTime();
      if (
        currentGroup &&
        currentGroup.isCurrentUser === isCurrentUser &&
        chat.sender?.id === currentGroup.senderId &&
        chatTime - currentGroup.lastTime < GROUP_TIME_WINDOW
      ) {
        currentGroup.messages.push(chat);
        currentGroup.lastTime = chatTime;
      } else {
        if (currentGroup) groups.push(currentGroup);
        currentGroup = {
          isCurrentUser,
          senderId: chat.sender?.id,
          senderName: chat.sender?.username || "Unknown",
          lastTime: chatTime,
          messages: [chat],
        };
      }
    });
    if (currentGroup) groups.push(currentGroup);
    return groups;
  }, [conversationHistory, currentUserId]);

  // Date separator positions
  const dateSeparators = useMemo(() => {
    const dates = new Map();
    conversationHistory.forEach((chat, index) => {
      const dateKey = chat.updatedAt
        ? new Date(chat.updatedAt).toDateString()
        : "unknown";
      if (!dates.has(dateKey)) {
        dates.set(dateKey, index);
      }
    });
    return dates;
  }, [conversationHistory]);

  const canDelete = (chat) => {
    return userRole === "ADMIN" || chat.sender?.id === currentUserId;
  };

  const handleAddToNotes = (chat) => {
    setSelectedChat(chat);
    setShowNoteModal(true);
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handleAddToTask = (chat) => {
    setSelectedChat(chat);
    setShowTaskModal(true);
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handleAddToList = (chat) => {
    setSelectedChat(chat);
    setSuggestionAction({ type: 'add_to_list', data: { chat } });
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handleDismissSuggestions = (messageId) => {
    setDismissedSuggestions((prev) => {
      const next = new Set(prev);
      next.add(messageId);
      return next;
    });
  };

  const handleSuggestionAction = (chat, type, data) => {
    setSelectedChat(chat);
    if (type === 'create_task') {
      setSuggestionAction({ type, data });
      setShowTaskModal(true);
    } else if (type === 'save_note') {
      setSuggestionAction({ type, data });
      setShowNoteModal(true);
    } else if (type === 'add_to_list') {
      setSuggestionAction({ type, data });
    } else if (type === 'save_snippet') {
      setSuggestionAction({ type, data });
    }
  };

  const handleReply = (chat) => {
    onReplyToChat?.(chat);
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handleForward = (chat) => {
    onForwardChat?.(chat);
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handleDirectMessage = (chat) => {
    onOpenDirectMessage?.(chat.sender);
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handleMoreInfo = (chat) => {
    setInfoChat(chat);
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handleCopyChatUrl = async (chat) => {
    const chatUrl = buildChatUrl(chat);
    if (!chatUrl) return;
    try {
      await navigator.clipboard.writeText(chatUrl);
    } catch {
      const textarea = document.createElement("textarea");
      textarea.value = chatUrl;
      document.body.appendChild(textarea);
      textarea.select();
      document.execCommand("copy");
      document.body.removeChild(textarea);
    }
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handleDelete = (chat) => {
    onDeleteChat(chat.id);
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const handlePin = (chat) => {
    onPinChat(chat.id, !chat.isPinned);
    setOpenOptionsId(null);
  };

  const isPinnedForCurrentUser = (chat) => {
    if (chat?.isPinnedForCurrentUser || chat?.isPinned) return true;
    return Array.isArray(chat?.taggedUsers) && chat.taggedUsers.some((tag) => tag.userId === currentUserId);
  };

  const isTaggedForCurrentUser = (chat) => {
    const tags = Array.isArray(chat?.taggedUsers) ? chat.taggedUsers : [];
    return tags.some((tag) => tag?.userId === currentUserId || tag?.user?.id === currentUserId);
  };

  const getReadStatusGroups = (chat) => {
    const senderId = chat.sender?.id;
    const receipts = Array.isArray(chat.readReceipts) ? chat.readReceipts : [];
    const nonSenderReceipts = receipts.filter((receipt) => receipt.user && receipt.user.id !== senderId);
    return {
      read: nonSenderReceipts
        .filter((receipt) => receipt.readAt)
        .sort((a, b) => new Date(a.readAt) - new Date(b.readAt)),
      unread: nonSenderReceipts.filter((receipt) => !receipt.readAt),
    };
  };

  const renderBubble = (chat, showSender, isLastInGroup) => {
    const isCurrentUser = chat.sender?.id === currentUserId;
    const isTagged = isTaggedForCurrentUser(chat);
    const time = formatTime(chat.updatedAt);
    const suggestions = !dismissedSuggestions.has(chat.id) ? getActionSuggestions(chat) : [];

    return (
      <div
        key={chat.id}
        ref={(el) => {
          if (chat.id) messageRefs.current[chat.id] = el;
        }}
        onMouseEnter={() => {
          if (chat.id && !chat.readReceipts?.find((r) => r.user?.id === currentUserId)) {
            markAsRead(chat.id);
          }
        }}
        className={`flex min-w-0 ${isCurrentUser ? "justify-end" : "justify-start"} ${isLastInGroup ? "mb-3" : "mb-0.5"}`}
      >
        <div className={`flex min-w-0 items-end group ${isCurrentUser ? "flex-row-reverse" : "flex-row"} gap-1.5 max-w-[92%] md:max-w-[82%] lg:max-w-[78%]`}>
          <div className="flex min-w-0 max-w-full flex-col">
            {showSender && !isCurrentUser && (
              <div className="chat-bubble-sender ml-1 mb-1">{chat.sender?.username || "Unknown"}</div>
            )}
            <div
              className={`chat-bubble relative ${
                isCurrentUser ? "chat-bubble-outgoing" : "chat-bubble-incoming"
              } ${isTagged ? "ring-2 ring-[var(--color-brand-border)] ring-offset-1 ring-offset-white" : ""} ${
                chat.isImportant && isCurrentUser ? "ring-1 ring-[var(--color-warning)]/50" : ""
              }`}
            >
              {isTagged && !isCurrentUser && (
                <span className="absolute -top-1.5 -left-1.5 bg-[var(--color-brand)] rounded-full p-0.5 shadow-sm" aria-label="You were tagged">
                  <AtSign size={10} className="text-white" />
                </span>
              )}
              {chat.isImportant && !isCurrentUser && (
                <Star size={12} className="absolute -top-1.5 -right-1.5 text-[var(--color-warning)] fill-current" />
              )}
              <div className="min-w-0 max-w-full break-words whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm leading-[1.45] [overflow-wrap:anywhere]">
                {renderChatContent(chat.contentHtml || chat.content)}
              </div>

              {chat.attachments && chat.attachments.length > 0 && (
                <div className={`mt-2 grid gap-1.5 ${
                  chat.attachments.length === 1
                    ? "grid-cols-1"
                    : chat.attachments.length === 2
                    ? "grid-cols-2"
                    : chat.attachments.length <= 4
                    ? "grid-cols-2"
                    : "grid-cols-3"
                }`}>
                  {chat.attachments.map((attachment) => (
                    <div key={attachment.id || attachment.url}>
                      {attachment.mimetype?.startsWith("image/") ? (
                        <div
                          className={`${
                            chat.attachments.length === 1
                              ? "chat-img-container"
                              : "rounded-lg overflow-hidden cursor-pointer aspect-square"
                          }`}
                          onClick={() => setLightboxImg(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}${attachment.url}`)}
                        >
                          <img
                            src={`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}${attachment.url}`}
                            alt={attachment.filename}
                            loading="lazy"
                            className={chat.attachments.length > 1 ? "w-full h-full object-cover" : ""}
                          />
                        </div>
                      ) : attachment.mimetype?.startsWith("video/") ? (
                        <video controls className="max-w-full h-auto rounded-lg">
                          <source src={attachment.url} type={attachment.mimetype} />
                        </video>
                      ) : (
                        <a
                          href={attachment.url}
                          target="_blank"
                          rel="noopener noreferrer"
                          className="underline text-white/80 hover:text-white text-sm"
                        >
                          {attachment.filename}
                        </a>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              )}

              <div className="chat-bubble-time">{time}</div>
            </div>

            {chat.requiresConfirmation &&
              !chat.readReceipts?.find((r) => r.user?.id === currentUserId && r.confirmedAt) &&
              !isCurrentUser && (
                <button
                  onClick={() => confirmRead(chat.id)}
                  className="confirm-btn mt-1 bg-[var(--color-danger)] text-white px-2 py-0.5 text-xs rounded-lg hover:opacity-90 self-start"
                >
                  Confirm Read
                </button>
              )}

            <ActionSuggestionBar
              suggestions={suggestions}
              messageId={chat.id}
              onAction={(type, data) => handleSuggestionAction(chat, type, data)}
              onDismiss={handleDismissSuggestions}
            />

            <ReactionsDisplay
              chatId={chat.id}
              reactions={reactionsMap[chat.id] || []}
              currentUserId={currentUserId}
              onReactionChange={handleReactionChange}
            />
          </div>

          {/* Options button */}
          <div className="relative flex-shrink-0 self-end">
            <button
              onClick={(e) => {
                e.stopPropagation();
                const rect = e.currentTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
                const menuWidth = 190;
                if (window.innerWidth - rect.right < menuWidth) {
                  setOptionsSide("left");
                } else {
                  setOptionsSide("right");
                }
                const estimatedMenuHeight = 320;
                const spaceBelow = window.innerHeight - rect.bottom;
                const spaceAbove = rect.top;
                if (spaceBelow < estimatedMenuHeight && spaceAbove >= spaceBelow) {
                  setOptionsVertical("up");
                } else {
                  setOptionsVertical("down");
                }
                setOpenOptionsId(isOpenOptions(chat.id) ? null : chat.id);
              }}
              className="chat-options-btn p-1 text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] rounded-lg hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] opacity-40 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity"
              aria-label="More options"
            >
              <MoreVertical size={16} />
            </button>

            {isOpenOptions(chat.id) && (
              <div
                className={`chat-options-menu absolute z-50 ${
                  optionsVertical === "down" ? "top-0" : "bottom-0"
                } ${
                  optionsSide === "right" ? "left-full ml-1" : "right-full mr-1"
                } w-48 max-h-[50vh] overflow-y-auto bg-[var(--color-surface)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] rounded-xl shadow-lg border border-[var(--color-border)] py-1 z-[90]`}
              >
                <button onClick={() => handleReply(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                  <Reply size={14} /> Reply to
                </button>
                <button onClick={() => handleForward(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                  <Forward size={14} /> Forward message
                </button>
                <button onClick={() => handleMoreInfo(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                  <Info size={14} /> More info
                </button>
                <button onClick={() => handleCopyChatUrl(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                  <Link2 size={14} /> Copy chat URL
                </button>
                {chat.sender?.id && chat.sender.id !== currentUserId && (
                  <button onClick={() => handleDirectMessage(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                    <MessageSquare size={14} /> Send private DM
                  </button>
                )}
                {orgPhoneNumber && chat.sender?.phoneNumber && chat.sender?.id !== currentUserId && (
                  <button
                    onClick={() => {
                      CallsService.makeCall(chat.sender.phoneNumber, orgPhoneNumber);
                      setOpenOptionsId(null);
                    }}
                    className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-[var(--color-success)]"
                  >
                    <Phone size={14} /> Call {chat.sender.username}
                  </button>
                )}
                <div className="border-t border-[var(--color-border)] my-1" />
                <button onClick={() => handleAddToNotes(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] text-sm">
                  Add to Notes
                </button>
                <button onClick={() => handleAddToTask(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] text-sm">
                  Add to Task
                </button>
                <button onClick={() => handleAddToList(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                  <List size={14} /> Add to List
                </button>
                {userRole === "ADMIN" && (
                  <>
                    <div className="border-t border-[var(--color-border)] my-1" />
                    <button onClick={() => handlePin(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                      <Pin size={14} /> {chat.isPinned ? "Unpin" : "Pin"}
                    </button>
                  </>
                )}
                {canDelete(chat) && (
                  <>
                    <div className="border-t border-[var(--color-border)] my-1" />
                    <button onClick={() => handleDelete(chat)} className="w-full text-left px-3 py-2 text-[var(--color-danger)] hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] flex items-center gap-2 text-sm">
                      <Trash2 size={14} /> Delete
                    </button>
                  </>
                )}
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const isOpenOptions = (chatId) => openOptionsId === chatId;

  return (
    <>
      <div className="chat-timeline" ref={timelineRef}>
        {showJumpLatest && conversationHistory.length > 0 && (
          <button onClick={scrollToLatest} className="chat-jump-latest" aria-label="Jump to latest message">
            <ChevronDown size={16} />
            Jump to latest
          </button>
        )}
        <div className="chat-timeline-inner relative">
          <AnimatePresence initial={false}>
            {groupedMessages.map((group, groupIndex) => {
              const firstMsg = group.messages[0];
              const dateLabel = formatDateLabel(firstMsg.updatedAt);
              const prevGroup = groupedMessages[groupIndex - 1];
              const prevDate = prevGroup ? formatDateLabel(prevGroup.messages[0]?.updatedAt) : null;
              const showDateSep = dateLabel && dateLabel !== prevDate;

              return (
                <React.Fragment key={firstMsg.id || `group-${groupIndex}`}>
                  {showDateSep && (
                    <motion.div
                      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 8 }}
                      animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
                      transition={{ duration: 0.2, ease: "easeOut" }}
                      className="chat-date-sep"
                    >
                      <span>{dateLabel}</span>
                    </motion.div>
                  )}
                  <motion.div
                    variants={groupVariants}
                    initial="initial"
                    animate="animate"
                    exit="exit"
                    className="chat-msg-group"
                  >
                    {group.messages.map((chat, msgIndex) => (
                      <motion.div
                        key={chat.id}
                        variants={bubbleVariants}
                        transition={{ type: "spring", stiffness: 400, damping: 28, mass: 0.8 }}
                        className={`relative ${isOpenOptions(chat.id) ? "z-[80]" : "z-0"}`}
                      >
                        {renderBubble(chat, msgIndex === 0, msgIndex === group.messages.length - 1)}
                      </motion.div>
                    ))}
                  </motion.div>
                </React.Fragment>
              );
            })}
          </AnimatePresence>
          <div ref={messagesEndRef} />
        </div>
      </div>

      {lightboxImg && (
        <div className="chat-lightbox" onClick={() => setLightboxImg(null)}>
          <img src={lightboxImg} alt="Preview" onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()} />
          <button
            onClick={() => setLightboxImg(null)}
            className="absolute top-4 right-4 text-white bg-black/50 rounded-full p-2 hover:bg-black/70 transition-colors"
            aria-label="Close preview"
          >
            <X size={24} />
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {showNoteModal && selectedChat && (
        <CreateNoteModal
          isOpen={showNoteModal}
          onClose={() => { setShowNoteModal(false); setSelectedChat(null); setSuggestionAction(null); }}
          onNoteCreated={() => { setShowNoteModal(false); setSelectedChat(null); setSuggestionAction(null); }}
          initialData={{
            title: suggestionAction?.data?.title || buildNoteTitle(selectedChat),
            content: suggestionAction?.data?.content || selectedChat.contentHtml || selectedChat.content,
            chat: selectedChat,
            chatUrl: buildChatUrl(selectedChat),
            chatSender: selectedChat?.sender?.username || "",
            chatRoomName: selectedChat?.chatRoom?.name || "",
            chatUpdatedAt: selectedChat?.updatedAt || "",
            firstSnippetContent: [
              "Copied from chat",
              `Sender: ${selectedChat?.sender?.username || "Unknown"}`,
              `Chat Room: ${selectedChat?.chatRoom?.name || "Unknown room"}`,
              selectedChat?.updatedAt ? `Sent: ${new Date(selectedChat.updatedAt).toLocaleString()}` : "",
              buildChatUrl(selectedChat) ? `Link: ${buildChatUrl(selectedChat)}` : "",
              "",
              stripHtmlTags(suggestionAction?.data?.content || selectedChat?.contentHtml || selectedChat?.content || ""),
            ].filter(Boolean).join("\n"),
          }}
        />
      )}

      {showTaskModal && selectedChat && (
        <CreateTaskModal
          isOpen={showTaskModal}
          onClose={() => { setShowTaskModal(false); setSelectedChat(null); setSuggestionAction(null); }}
          onTaskCreated={() => { setShowTaskModal(false); setSelectedChat(null); setSuggestionAction(null); }}
          initialData={{
            title: suggestionAction?.data?.title || buildTaskTitle(selectedChat),
            content: buildQuotedHtml(selectedChat),
            chat: selectedChat,
            chatUrl: buildChatUrl(selectedChat),
            chatSender: selectedChat?.sender?.username || "",
            chatRoomName: selectedChat?.chatRoom?.name || "",
            chatUpdatedAt: selectedChat?.updatedAt || "",
          }}
        />
      )}

      {infoChat && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 z-[1000] flex items-center justify-center bg-black/60 p-4">
          <div className="w-full max-w-md rounded-xl bg-[var(--color-surface)] text-[var(--color-text-primary)] shadow-xl border border-[var(--color-border)]">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between border-b border-[var(--color-border)] px-4 py-3">
              <div>
                <h3 className="text-base font-semibold">Message info</h3>
                <p className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">
                  {infoChat.sender?.username || "Unknown"} &bull; {formatTime(infoChat.updatedAt)}
                </p>
              </div>
              <button type="button" onClick={() => setInfoChat(null)} className="flex h-8 w-8 items-center justify-center rounded-lg hover:bg-[var(--color-surface-muted)] text-[var(--color-text-muted)]" aria-label="Close message info">
                <X size={16} />
              </button>
            </div>
            <div className="max-h-[70vh] overflow-y-auto px-4 py-4">
              {(() => {
                const { read, unread } = getReadStatusGroups(infoChat);
                return (
                  <div className="space-y-5">
                    <section>
                      <div className="mb-2 flex items-center gap-2 font-semibold text-[var(--color-success)]">
                        <CheckCheck size={16} />
                        Read ({read.length})
                      </div>
                      {read.length > 0 ? (
                        <ul className="space-y-2">
                          {read.map((receipt) => (
                            <li key={receipt.id || receipt.user.id} className="rounded-lg bg-[var(--color-bg)] px-3 py-2 border border-[var(--color-border)]">
                              <div className="font-medium text-[var(--color-text-primary)]">{receipt.user.username || "Unknown"}</div>
                              <div className="text-xs text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">{new Date(receipt.readAt).toLocaleString()}</div>
                            </li>
                          ))}
                        </ul>
                      ) : (
                        <p className="text-sm text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">No one has read this yet.</p>
                      )}
                    </section>
                    <section>
                      <div className="mb-2 font-semibold text-[var(--color-text-secondary)]">Unread ({unread.length})</div>
                      {unread.length > 0 ? (
                        <ul className="space-y-2">
                          {unread.map((receipt) => (
                            <li key={receipt.id || receipt.user.id} className="rounded-lg bg-[var(--color-bg)] px-3 py-2 border border-[var(--color-border)]">
                              <div className="font-medium text-[var(--color-text-primary)]">{receipt.user.username || "Unknown"}</div>
                            </li>
                          ))}
                        </ul>
                      ) : (
                        <p className="text-sm text-[var(--color-text-muted)]">Everyone with a receipt has read this.</p>
                      )}
                    </section>
                  </div>
                );
              })()}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </>
  );
};

ConversationList.propTypes = {
  conversationHistory: PropTypes.array.isRequired,
  currentUserId: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
  userRole: PropTypes.string,
  markAsRead: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  confirmRead: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  onDeleteChat: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  onPinChat: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
  onReplyToChat: PropTypes.func,
  onForwardChat: PropTypes.func,
  onOpenDirectMessage: PropTypes.func,
  scrollToMessageId: PropTypes.string,
  scrollToMessageRequestToken: PropTypes.number,
  selectedThread: PropTypes.string,
};

export default ConversationList;

```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/EmojiPicker.jsx
import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from "react";
import data from "@emoji-mart/data";
import Picker from "@emoji-mart/react";

const EmojiPicker = ({ onSelect, onClose, align = "left" }) => {
  const ref = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleClickOutside = (e) => {
      if (ref.current && !ref.current.contains(e.target)) {
        onClose();
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
  }, [onClose]);

  return (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      className={`absolute bottom-full mb-2 z-50 ${align === "right" ? "right-0" : "left-0"}`}
      style={{ width: "min(352px, calc(100vw - 32px))" }}
    >
      <Picker
        data={data}
        onEmojiSelect={(emoji) => onSelect(emoji.native || emoji.id)}
        theme="light"
        previewPosition="none"
        skinTonePosition="search"
        set="native"
        maxFrequentRows={1}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

export default EmojiPicker;
```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ImportantChatManager.jsx
// client/services/chat/components/ImportantChatManager.js
import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from 'react';
import { AuthContext } from '@/shared/context/AuthContext';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import ImportantChatPopup from './ImportantChatPopup';
import { useGenericSocket } from '@/shared/hooks/useGenericSocket';

const ImportantChatManager = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);
  const [importantChats, setImportantChats] = useState([]);
  const [currentChatIndex, setCurrentChatIndex] = useState(0);
  const { socket } = useGenericSocket('chat');

  useEffect(() => {
    const fetchImportantChats = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetchWithAuth(
          `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chats/important/active`
        );
        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json();
          setImportantChats(data.importantChats);
          setCurrentChatIndex(0);
        }
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Failed to fetch important chats", error);
      }
    };

    if (user) {
      fetchImportantChats();
    }
  }, [user]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (socket && user) {
        const handleNewImportantChat = (chat) => {
            setImportantChats(prev => {
                if (prev.some(c => c.id === chat.id)) return prev;
                return [chat, ...prev];
            });
            setCurrentChatIndex(0);
        };

        socket.on('importantChatSet', handleNewImportantChat);

        return () => {
            socket.off('importantChatSet', handleNewImportantChat);
        };
    }
  }, [socket, user]);

  const handleClosePopup = () => {
    if (currentChatIndex < importantChats.length - 1) {
      setCurrentChatIndex(currentChatIndex + 1);
    } else {
      setImportantChats([]);
    }
  };

  if (!user || importantChats.length === 0 || currentChatIndex >= importantChats.length) {
    return null;
  }

  return (
    <ImportantChatPopup
      chat={importantChats[currentChatIndex]}
      onClose={handleClosePopup}
    />
  );
};

export default ImportantChatManager;
```

FILE: client/services/chat/components/ImportantChatPopup.jsx

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ImportantChatPopup.jsx
import React from 'react';
import PropTypes from 'prop-types';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { useRouter } from 'next/router';

const ImportantChatPopup = ({ chat, onClose }) => {
  const router = useRouter();

  const handleConfirm = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chats/${chat.id}/confirm-important`,
        { method: 'PUT' }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || 'Failed to confirm announcement.');
      }
      toast.success('Announcement confirmed.');
      onClose();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Confirm Announcement Error:', error);
      toast.error(error.message);
    }
  };

  const handleGoToChat = async () => {
    // Navigate first
    router.push(`/chat?chatRoomId=${chat.chatRoom.id}&threadId=${chat.thread.id}`);
    
    // Then try to confirm and close the popup
    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/chats/${chat.id}/confirm-important`,
        { method: 'PUT' }
      );
      if (!res.ok) {
        toast.error('Failed to confirm announcement.');
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Confirm Announcement Error:', error);
      toast.error(error.message);
    } finally {
      onClose();
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-60 flex items-center justify-center z-[100] p-4">
      <div className="bg-white rounded-lg shadow-2xl w-full max-w-md flex flex-col max-h-[calc(100vh-2rem)]">
        <div className="p-6 overflow-y-auto">
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-4 text-primary">Important Announcement</h2>
          <div className="p-4 bg-gray-100 rounded-md">
            <p className="font-semibold text-gray-800">{chat.sender.username} says:</p>
            <p className="text-gray-700 mt-2 whitespace-pre-wrap">{chat.content}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="px-6 pb-6 pt-4 flex-shrink-0 border-t border-gray-200">
          <div className="flex justify-between items-center space-x-4">
            <button
              onClick={handleGoToChat}
              className="btn btn-primary flex-1"
            >
              Go to Chat
            </button>
            <button
              onClick={handleConfirm}
              className="btn btn-secondary flex-1"
            >
              Confirm Read
            </button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

ImportantChatPopup.propTypes = {
  chat: PropTypes.shape({
    id: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
    content: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
    chatRoom: PropTypes.shape({
      id: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
    }).isRequired,
    thread: PropTypes.shape({
      id: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
    }).isRequired,
    sender: PropTypes.shape({
      username: PropTypes.string.isRequired,
    }).isRequired,
  }).isRequired,
  onClose: PropTypes.func.isRequired,
};

export default ImportantChatPopup;
```

FILE: client/services/chat/components/MentionAlertManager.jsx

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/MentionAlertManager.jsx
import React, { useCallback, useContext, useEffect, useMemo, useState } from 'react';
import { useRouter } from 'next/router';
import { AtSign, CheckCircle2, ChevronDown, X } from 'lucide-react';
import { toast } from 'react-toastify';
import { AuthContext } from '@/shared/context/AuthContext';
import { fetchWithAuth } from '@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth';
import { useGenericSocket } from '@/shared/hooks/useGenericSocket';

const stripHtmlForPreview = (value = '') =>
  String(value || '')
    .replace(/<br\s*\/?>/gi, '\n')
    .replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '')
    .trim();

const isTaggedForUser = (chat, userId) => {
  const tags = Array.isArray(chat?.taggedUsers) ? chat.taggedUsers : [];
  return tags.some((tag) => tag?.userId === userId || tag?.user?.id === userId);
};

const getChatTarget = (chat) => ({
  roomId: chat?.thread?.chatRoomId || chat?.chatRoom?.id || chat?.chatRoomId,
  threadId: chat?.thread?.id || chat?.threadId,
  messageId: chat?.id,
});

const MentionAlertManager = () => {
  const { user } = useContext(AuthContext);
  const { socket } = useGenericSocket('chat');
  const router = useRouter();
  const [mentions, setMentions] = useState([]);
  const [activeIndex, setActiveIndex] = useState(0);

  const shouldShow = user && router.pathname !== '/chat' && mentions.length > 0;

  const activeMention = useMemo(() => {
    if (mentions.length === 0) return null;
    return mentions[Math.min(activeIndex, mentions.length - 1)] || null;
  }, [activeIndex, mentions]);

  const fetchMentions = useCallback(async () => {
    if (!user?.id) return;

    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/widget`);
      if (!res.ok) return;
      const data = await res.json();
      const tagged = (Array.isArray(data.pinnedChats) ? data.pinnedChats : [])
        .filter((chat) => isTaggedForUser(chat, user.id));
      setMentions(tagged);
      setActiveIndex(0);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Fetch mention alerts error:', error);
    }
  }, [user?.id]);

  useEffect(() => {
    fetchMentions();
  }, [fetchMentions]);

  const openMention = useCallback((chat = activeMention) => {
    const { roomId, threadId, messageId } = getChatTarget(chat);
    if (!roomId || !threadId || !messageId) return;

    router.push(
      `/chat?chatRoomId=${encodeURIComponent(roomId)}&threadId=${encodeURIComponent(threadId)}&messageId=${encodeURIComponent(messageId)}`
    );
  }, [activeMention, router]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!socket || !user?.id) return undefined;

    const handleNewChat = (chat) => {
      if (!isTaggedForUser(chat, user.id) || chat?.sender?.id === user.id) return;

      setMentions((prev) => {
        if (prev.some((item) => item.id === chat.id)) return prev;
        return [chat, ...prev];
      });
      setActiveIndex(0);

      toast.warn(`${chat?.sender?.username || 'Someone'} mentioned you`, {
        autoClose: 10000,
        onClick: () => openMention(chat),
      });
    };

    socket.on('newChat', handleNewChat);
    socket.on('chatUpdated', fetchMentions);
    socket.on('chatDeleted', fetchMentions);

    return () => {
      socket.off('newChat', handleNewChat);
      socket.off('chatUpdated', fetchMentions);
      socket.off('chatDeleted', fetchMentions);
    };
  }, [fetchMentions, openMention, socket, user?.id]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeIndex > mentions.length - 1) {
      setActiveIndex(0);
    }
  }, [activeIndex, mentions.length]);

  const dismissMention = async (chat = activeMention) => {
    if (!chat?.id) return;
    setMentions((prev) => prev.filter((item) => item.id !== chat.id));

    try {
      await fetchWithAuth(
        `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/widget/${chat.id}/dismiss`,
        { method: 'PUT' }
      );
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Dismiss mention alert error:', error);
      fetchMentions();
    }
  };

  if (!shouldShow || !activeMention) {
    return null;
  }

  const preview = stripHtmlForPreview(activeMention.content);
  const roomName = activeMention?.chatRoom?.name || 'Chat';
  const senderName = activeMention?.sender?.username || 'Someone';

  return (
    <div className="fixed bottom-4 left-4 right-4 z-[70] sm:left-auto sm:right-4 sm:w-[24rem]">
      <div className="overflow-hidden rounded-xl border border-[#d9ccff] bg-white shadow-2xl">
        <div className="flex items-start gap-3 bg-[#f0ebff] px-4 py-3 text-[#312e81]">
          <div className="mt-0.5 flex h-9 w-9 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-full bg-[#6b4bd8] text-white">
            <AtSign size={17} />
          </div>
          <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-semibold">
              <span>Priority mention</span>
              {mentions.length > 1 && (
                <span className="rounded-full bg-[#d9ccff] px-2 py-0.5 text-xs">
                  {Math.min(activeIndex, mentions.length - 1) + 1}/{mentions.length}
                </span>
              )}
            </div>
            <div className="mt-0.5 text-xs text-[#4338ca]/80">
              {roomName} · {senderName}
            </div>
            <div className="mt-1 line-clamp-2 text-sm text-[#312e81]">
              {preview || 'Open chat to view the message.'}
            </div>
          </div>
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setMentions([])}
            className="flex h-8 w-8 shrink-0 items-center justify-center rounded-lg text-[#4338ca]/70 hover:bg-white/60"
            aria-label="Hide mention alerts"
            title="Hide"
          >
            <X size={16} />
          </button>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center justify-end gap-2 border-t border-[#d9ccff] px-3 py-2">
          {mentions.length > 1 && (
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setActiveIndex((index) => (index + 1) % mentions.length)}
              className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold text-[#6b4bd8] hover:bg-[#f0ebff]"
            >
              <ChevronDown size={14} />
              Next
            </button>
          )}
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => dismissMention()}
            className="inline-flex items-center gap-1.5 rounded-lg px-2.5 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold text-base-content/60 hover:bg-base-200"
          >
            <CheckCircle2 size={14} />
            Done
          </button>
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => openMention()}
            className="rounded-lg bg-[#6b4bd8] px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-semibold text-white hover:bg-[#5438df]"
          >
            View
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default MentionAlertManager;

```

FILE: client/services/chat/components/ReactionsDisplay.jsx
