```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/ReactionsDisplay.jsx
import React, { useState, useRef, useEffect } from "react";
import { SmilePlus, X } from "lucide-react";
import { fetchWithAuth } from "@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth";
import EmojiPicker from "./EmojiPicker";

const QUICK_REACTIONS = ["👍", "❤️", "😂", "👀", "✅"];

const ReactionsDisplay = ({
  chatId,
  reactions = [],
  currentUserId,
  onReactionChange,
}) => {
  const [showQuickPicker, setShowQuickPicker] = useState(false);
  const [showFullPicker, setShowFullPicker] = useState(false);
  const pickerRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleClickOutside = (e) => {
      if (pickerRef.current && !pickerRef.current.contains(e.target)) {
        setShowQuickPicker(false);
        setShowFullPicker(false);
      }
    };
    document.addEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
    return () => document.removeEventListener("mousedown", handleClickOutside);
  }, []);

  const grouped = {};
  reactions.forEach((r) => {
    if (!grouped[r.emoji]) grouped[r.emoji] = [];
    grouped[r.emoji].push(r);
  });

  const hasReacted = (emoji) =>
    reactions.some((r) => r.emoji === emoji && r.user?.id === currentUserId);

  const toggleReaction = async (emoji) => {
    setShowQuickPicker(false);
    setShowFullPicker(false);

    try {
      if (hasReacted(emoji)) {
        const res = await fetchWithAuth(
          `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/reactions/${chatId}/${encodeURIComponent(emoji)}`,
          { method: "DELETE" }
        );
        if (res.ok && onReactionChange) {
          onReactionChange({ type: "remove", chatId, emoji, userId: currentUserId });
        }
      } else {
        const res = await fetchWithAuth(
          `${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/chat/reactions`,
          {
            method: "POST",
            headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
            body: JSON.stringify({ chatId, emoji }),
          }
        );
        if (res.ok && onReactionChange) {
          const data = await res.json();
          onReactionChange({ type: "add", chatId, reaction: data.reaction });
        }
      }
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Reaction error:", err);
    }
  };

  if (!reactions || reactions.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="relative" ref={pickerRef}>
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={() => setShowQuickPicker(!showQuickPicker)}
          className="flex items-center gap-1 mt-1 text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] transition-colors text-xs px-0.5"
          title="Add reaction"
        >
          <SmilePlus size={14} />
        </button>
        {showQuickPicker && (
          <div className="absolute bottom-full left-0 mb-1 flex gap-1 bg-[var(--color-surface)] border border-[var(--color-border)] rounded-lg shadow-lg p-1.5 z-50">
            {QUICK_REACTIONS.map((emoji) => (
              <button
                key={emoji}
                type="button"
                onClick={() => toggleReaction(emoji)}
                className="text-lg hover:scale-125 transition-transform p-0.5"
              >
                {emoji}
              </button>
            ))}
            <div className="w-px bg-[var(--color-border)] mx-0.5" />
            <button
              type="button"
              onClick={() => setShowFullPicker(true)}
              className="text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] p-0.5"
              title="More emojis"
            >
              <SmilePlus size={14} />
            </button>
            {showFullPicker && (
              <div className="absolute bottom-full left-0 mb-1" style={{ width: "300px" }}>
                <EmojiPicker
                  onSelect={(emoji) => toggleReaction(emoji)}
                  onClose={() => setShowFullPicker(false)}
                />
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        )}
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="relative" ref={pickerRef}>
      <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 mt-1">
        {Object.entries(grouped).map(([emoji, users]) => (
          <button
            key={emoji}
            type="button"
            onClick={() => toggleReaction(emoji)}
            className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs border transition-all ${
              hasReacted(emoji)
                ? "bg-[var(--color-brand-light)] border-[var(--color-brand-border)]"
                : "bg-[var(--color-bg)] border-[var(--color-border)] hover:border-[var(--color-brand-border)]"
            }`}
          >
            <span className="text-sm leading-none">{emoji}</span>
            <span className="text-[var(--color-text-muted)] font-medium">{users.length}</span>
          </button>
        ))}
        <button
          type="button"
          onClick={() => setShowQuickPicker(!showQuickPicker)}
          className="inline-flex items-center px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs border border-[var(--color-border)] bg-[var(--color-bg)] hover:border-[var(--color-brand-border)] text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] transition-all"
          title="Add reaction"
        >
          <SmilePlus size={12} />
        </button>
      </div>
      {showQuickPicker && (
        <div className="absolute bottom-full left-0 mb-1 flex gap-1 bg-[var(--color-surface)] border border-[var(--color-border)] rounded-lg shadow-lg p-1.5 z-50">
          {QUICK_REACTIONS.map((emoji) => (
            <button
              key={emoji}
              type="button"
              onClick={() => toggleReaction(emoji)}
              className="text-lg hover:scale-125 transition-transform p-0.5"
            >
              {emoji}
            </button>
          ))}
          <div className="w-px bg-[var(--color-border)] mx-0.5" />
          <button
            type="button"
            onClick={() => setShowFullPicker(true)}
            className="text-[var(--color-text-muted)] hover:text-[var(--color-text-secondary)] p-0.5"
          >
            <SmilePlus size={14} />
          </button>
          {showFullPicker && (
            <div className="absolute bottom-full left-0 mb-1" style={{ width: "300px" }}>
              <EmojiPicker
                onSelect={(emoji) => toggleReaction(emoji)}
                onClose={() => setShowFullPicker(false)}
              />
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
};

export default ReactionsDisplay;

```

```jsx
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/components/StatusDropdown.jsx
//--- File: client/services/chat/components/StatusDropdown.js ---
import React, { useState, useContext } from "react";
import { AuthContext } from "@/shared/context/AuthContext";
import { fetchWithAuth } from "@/shared/utils/fetchWithAuth";
import { toast } from "react-toastify";

const StatusDropdown = () => {
  const { user, setUser } = useContext(AuthContext);
  const [currentStatus, setCurrentStatus] = useState(user?.status || "OFFLINE");

  const statuses = ["ONLINE", "BUSY", "OFFLINE", "AWAY"];

  const handleChangeStatus = async (e) => {
    const newStatus = e.target.value;
    setCurrentStatus(newStatus);

    try {
      const res = await fetchWithAuth(`${process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_SERVER_URL}/user/status`, {
        method: "PUT",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ status: newStatus }),
      });
      if (!res.ok) {
        const errorData = await res.json();
        throw new Error(errorData.error || "Failed to update status.");
      }
      const data = await res.json();
      // Update local user context
      setUser({ ...user, status: data.user.status });
      toast.success("Status updated!");
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
      toast.error(error.message);
    }
  };

  return (
    <select value={currentStatus} onChange={handleChangeStatus} className="border p-1 rounded">
      {statuses.map((s) => (
        <option key={s} value={s}>{s}</option>
      ))}
    </select>
  );
};

export default StatusDropdown;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/client/services/chat/utils/tests/actionSuggestions.test.js
import { getActionSuggestions } from '../actionSuggestions';

describe('getActionSuggestions', () => {
  it('returns empty array for empty text', () => {
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: '' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: '   ' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({})).toEqual([]);
  });

  it('returns empty for very short messages', () => {
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'ok' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'hi' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'lol' })).toEqual([]);
  });

  it('returns empty for emoji-only messages', () => {
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: '👍' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: '🚀🔥' })).toEqual([]);
  });

  it('returns empty for casual replies', () => {
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'thanks' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'sure' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'yes' })).toEqual([]);
  });

  it('suggests create_task for todo-like messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Todo: review the Q3 report' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'create_task')).toBe(true);
    expect(result[0].confidence).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(0.3);
  });

  it('suggests create_task for "follow up" messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Please follow up with the client about the contract' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'create_task')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests create_task for task assignment messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Can someone assign this to John? Due by Friday.' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'create_task')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests create_task for deadline messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Need to finish the proposal by tomorrow EOD' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'create_task')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests save_note for note-like messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Important note: The server password rotation policy is every 90 days' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'save_note')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests save_note for reference messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'For reference, the API base URL is https://api.example.com/v2' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'save_note')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests save_note for FYI messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'FYI - The deployment instructions are in the wiki' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'save_note')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests save_note for policy messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Company policy: All PRs require two reviewers' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'save_note')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests add_to_list for shopping/grocery messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'We need to add to list: milk, eggs, bread, and butter' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'add_to_list')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests add_to_list for bullet item lists', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({
      content: '- Apples\n- Bananas\n- 3x Oranges\n- 2 cases of water',
    });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'add_to_list')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests add_to_list for quantity-based messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Need to order: 5 boxes of paper, 10 units of toner' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'add_to_list')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests save_snippet for procedure messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Steps to deploy: 1. Run tests 2. Build 3. Deploy to staging' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'save_snippet')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('suggests save_snippet for template messages', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Here is the template for bug reports: ## Summary ## Steps to Reproduce ## Expected Behavior' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'save_snippet')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('returns multiple suggestions when multiple signals match', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({
      content: 'Remember to follow up on the Q3 review. Steps: 1. Review metrics 2. Schedule meeting 3. Send summary',
    });
    expect(result.length).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(2);
  });

  it('returns at most 3 suggestions', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({
      content: 'Todo: review. Note: important. Add to list: milk, eggs. Procedure: deploy. FYI: reference doc.',
    });
    expect(result.length).toBeLessThanOrEqual(3);
  });

  it('penalizes reply messages', () => {
    const direct = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Todo: finish the report' });
    const reply = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Todo: finish the report' }, { isReply: true });
    if (direct.length > 0 && reply.length > 0) {
      expect(reply[0].confidence).toBeLessThan(direct[0].confidence);
    }
  });

  it('uses contentHtml if content is empty', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ contentHtml: '<p>Todo: fix the login bug</p>' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'create_task')).toBe(true);
  });

  it('infers title from first line of content', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({ content: 'Todo: review the quarterly report\nThis is a long message with additional details' });
    expect(result.some(s => s.type === 'create_task')).toBe(true);
    const taskSugg = result.find(s => s.type === 'create_task');
    expect(taskSugg.data.title).toBe('Todo: review the quarterly report');
  });

  it('returns empty for normal conversational messages', () => {
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'How is everyone doing today?' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'That sounds great!' })).toEqual([]);
    expect(getActionSuggestions({ content: 'I agree with what you said' })).toEqual([]);
  });

  it('sorts by confidence descending', () => {
    const result = getActionSuggestions({
      content: 'Todo: finish the project. Note: important reference. Add 3x milk, 2 cases of water to shopping list.',
    });
    for (let i = 1; i < result.length; i++) {
      expect(result[i - 1].confidence).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(result[i].confidence);
    }
  });
});
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/chatRooms.js
import express from "express";
import prisma from "#shared/database/prismaClient.js";
import withHandler from "#shared/utils/withHandler.js";
import { getNamespace } from "#shared/socket.js";

const router = express.Router();

const SUPPORT_USER_ID = "cm5et7qvf0001yqc7k5j0e9sl";

const canManagePublicRooms = (user) =>
  user?.role === "ADMIN" || user?.id === SUPPORT_USER_ID;

const canDeleteChatRoom = ({ user, chatRoom }) => {
  if (!user || !chatRoom) return false;

  if (canManagePublicRooms(user)) return true;

  if (!chatRoom.isPrivate) return false;

  return chatRoom.participants.some((participant) => participant.id === user.id);
};

const getIsMutedForUser = ({ chatRoom, mutedByCurrentUser }) => {
  if (chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
    // Site-wide rooms are muted by default.
    // A record means the user explicitly opted in to notifications.
    return mutedByCurrentUser.length === 0;
  }

  return mutedByCurrentUser.length > 0;
};

const createChatRoom = async (req, res) => {
  const { name, description, isPrivate, participantIds, shiftNotify } = req.body;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  if (!name) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Chatroom name is required." });
  }

  try {
    let participants = { connect: { id: userId } };

    if (isPrivate) {
      if (
        participantIds &&
        Array.isArray(participantIds) &&
        participantIds.length > 0
      ) {
        if (!participantIds.includes(userId)) {
          participantIds.push(userId);
        }
        participants = {
          connect: participantIds.map((id) => ({ id })),
        };
      } else {
        participants = { connect: { id: userId } };
      }
    }

    const newChatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.create({
      data: {
        name,
        description: description || null,
        isPrivate: isPrivate || false,
        shiftNotify: Boolean(shiftNotify),
        organization: organizationId
          ? { connect: { id: organizationId } }
          : undefined,
        participants,
        threads: {
          create: {
            title: "General",
          },
        },
      },
      include: {
        threads: true,
        participants: {
          select: {
            id: true,
            username: true,
            email: true,
          },
        },
        mutedBy: {
          where: {
            userId,
          },
          select: { userId: true },
        },
      },
    });

    const chatRoomForResponse = {
      ...newChatRoom,
      isMuted: getIsMutedForUser({
        chatRoom: newChatRoom,
        mutedByCurrentUser: newChatRoom.mutedBy || [],
      }),
    };

    delete chatRoomForResponse.mutedBy;

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");
    if (organizationId) {
      chatNamespace.to(`org_${organizationId}`).emit("newChatRoom", chatRoomForResponse);
    } else {
      chatNamespace.to("site_wide_room").emit("newChatRoom", chatRoomForResponse);
    }

    res.status(201).json({ chatRoom: chatRoomForResponse });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Create ChatRoom Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const getChatRooms = async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  try {
    const baseWhere = {
      AND: [
        {
          OR: [{ organizationId: organizationId }, { organizationId: null }],
        },
        {
          OR: [
            { isPrivate: false },
            { isPrivate: true, participants: { some: { id: userId } } },
          ],
        },
      ],
    };

    const chatRoomsData = await prisma.chatRoom.findMany({
      where: baseWhere,
      include: {
        threads: true,
        participants: {
          select: {
            id: true,
            username: true,
            email: true,
          },
        },
        mutedBy: {
          where: {
            userId: userId,
          },
          select: { userId: true },
        },
      },
      orderBy: {
        updatedAt: "desc",
      },
    });

    const chatRooms = chatRoomsData.map((room) => {
      const isMuted = getIsMutedForUser({
        chatRoom: room,
        mutedByCurrentUser: room.mutedBy || [],
      });

      const { mutedBy, ...rest } = room;
      return { ...rest, isMuted };
    });

    res.status(200).json({ chatRooms });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Get ChatRooms Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal Server Error." });
  }
};

const getChatRoomById = async (req, res) => {
  const { id } = req.params;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  if (!id) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Chatroom ID is required." });
  }

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: {
        participants: {
          select: {
            id: true,
            username: true,
            email: true,
            phoneNumber: true,
          },
        },
        mutedBy: {
          where: {
            userId,
          },
          select: { userId: true },
        },
      },
    });

    if (!chatRoom) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chatroom not found." });
    }

    if (
      chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
      chatRoom.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chatroom." });
    }

    if (chatRoom.isPrivate) {
      const isParticipant = chatRoom.participants.some(
        (participant) => participant.id === userId
      );
      if (!isParticipant) {
        return res
          .status(403)
          .json({ error: "You are not a participant of this chatroom." });
      }
    }

    const chatRoomForResponse = {
      ...chatRoom,
      isMuted: getIsMutedForUser({
        chatRoom,
        mutedByCurrentUser: chatRoom.mutedBy || [],
      }),
    };

    delete chatRoomForResponse.mutedBy;

    res.status(200).json({ chatRoom: chatRoomForResponse });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Get ChatRoom Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const getChatRoomMentionUsers = async (req, res) => {
  const { id } = req.params;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  if (!id) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Chatroom ID is required." });
  }

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: {
        participants: {
          select: {
            id: true,
            username: true,
            email: true,
            firstName: true,
            lastName: true,
            active: true,
          },
        },
      },
    });

    if (!chatRoom) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chatroom not found." });
    }

    if (
      chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
      chatRoom.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chatroom." });
    }

    if (chatRoom.isPrivate) {
      const isParticipant = chatRoom.participants.some(
        (participant) => participant.id === userId
      );

      if (!isParticipant) {
        return res
          .status(403)
          .json({ error: "You are not a participant of this chatroom." });
      }

      return res.status(200).json({
        users: chatRoom.participants.filter((participant) => participant.active !== false),
      });
    }

    const users = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where:
        chatRoom.organizationId === null
          ? { active: true }
          : { organizationId: chatRoom.organizationId, active: true },
      select: {
        id: true,
        username: true,
        email: true,
        firstName: true,
        lastName: true,
        active: true,
      },
      orderBy: {
        username: "asc",
      },
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ users });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Get ChatRoom Mention Users Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const updateChatRoom = async (req, res) => {
  const { id } = req.params;
  const { name, description, isPrivate, participantIds, shiftNotify } = req.body;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;

  if (!id) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Chatroom ID is required." });
  }

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: { participants: true },
    });

    if (!chatRoom) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chatroom not found." });
    }

    if (
      chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
      chatRoom.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chatroom." });
    }

    if (!canManagePublicRooms(req.user)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Only admins can edit chatrooms." });
    }

    const updatedChatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.update({
      where: { id },
      data: {
        name: name ?? chatRoom.name,
        description: description !== undefined ? description : chatRoom.description,
        isPrivate: isPrivate !== undefined ? isPrivate : chatRoom.isPrivate,
        shiftNotify:
          typeof shiftNotify === "boolean" ? shiftNotify : chatRoom.shiftNotify,
        participants: participantIds
          ? {
              set: participantIds.map((pid) => ({ id: pid })),
            }
          : undefined,
      },
      include: {
        participants: {
          select: {
            id: true,
            username: true,
            email: true,
          },
        },
        threads: true,
        mutedBy: {
          where: {
            userId,
          },
          select: { userId: true },
        },
      },
    });

    const chatRoomForResponse = {
      ...updatedChatRoom,
      isMuted: getIsMutedForUser({
        chatRoom: updatedChatRoom,
        mutedByCurrentUser: updatedChatRoom.mutedBy || [],
      }),
    };

    delete chatRoomForResponse.mutedBy;

    res.status(200).json({ chatRoom: chatRoomForResponse });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Update ChatRoom Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const deleteChatRoom = async (req, res) => {
  const { id } = req.params;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  if (!id) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Chatroom ID is required." });
  }

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id },
      include: { participants: true },
    });

    if (!chatRoom) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chatroom not found." });
    }

    if (
      chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
      chatRoom.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chatroom." });
    }

    const allowedToDelete = canDeleteChatRoom({
      user: req.user,
      chatRoom,
    });

    if (!allowedToDelete) {
      return res.status(403).json({
        error: "You do not have permission to delete this chatroom.",
      });
    }

    await prisma.chatRoom.delete({
      where: { id },
    });

    res.status(200).json({ message: "Chatroom deleted successfully." });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Delete ChatRoom Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const toggleMuteChatRoom = async (req, res) => {
  const { id } = req.params;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({ where: { id } });
    if (!chatRoom) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chatroom not found." });
    }

    const existingMute = await prisma.userMutedChatRoom.findUnique({
      where: {
        userId_chatRoomId: {
          userId,
          chatRoomId: id,
        },
      },
    });

    if (chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
      // Site-wide rooms are muted by default.
      // Presence of a row means notifications are enabled.
      if (existingMute) {
        await prisma.userMutedChatRoom.delete({
          where: {
            userId_chatRoomId: {
              userId,
              chatRoomId: id,
            },
          },
        });

        return res.status(200).json({
          message: "Site-wide chat notifications muted.",
          isMuted: true,
        });
      }

      await prisma.userMutedChatRoom.create({
        data: {
          userId,
          chatRoomId: id,
        },
      });

      return res.status(200).json({
        message: "Site-wide chat notifications enabled.",
        isMuted: false,
      });
    }

    if (existingMute) {
      await prisma.userMutedChatRoom.delete({
        where: {
          userId_chatRoomId: {
            userId,
            chatRoomId: id,
          },
        },
      });
      return res
        .status(200)
        .json({ message: "Chatroom unmuted successfully.", isMuted: false });
    }

    await prisma.userMutedChatRoom.create({
      data: {
        userId,
        chatRoomId: id,
      },
    });

    return res
      .status(200)
      .json({ message: "Chatroom muted successfully.", isMuted: true });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Toggle Mute ChatRoom Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

router.put(
  "/:id",
  withHandler({
    handler: updateChatRoom,
    allowedMethods: ["PUT"],
  })
);

router.delete(
  "/:id",
  withHandler({
    handler: deleteChatRoom,
    allowedMethods: ["DELETE"],
  })
);

router.put(
  "/:id/mute",
  withHandler({
    handler: toggleMuteChatRoom,
    allowedMethods: ["PUT"],
  })
);

router.post(
  "/",
  withHandler({
    handler: createChatRoom,
    allowedMethods: ["POST"],
  })
);

router.get(
  "/",
  withHandler({
    handler: getChatRooms,
    allowedMethods: ["GET"],
  })
);

router.get(
  "/:id/mention-users",
  withHandler({
    handler: getChatRoomMentionUsers,
    allowedMethods: ["GET"],
  })
);

router.get(
  "/:id",
  withHandler({
    handler: getChatRoomById,
    allowedMethods: ["GET"],
  })
);

export default router;

```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/chats.js
import express from "express";
import prisma from "#shared/database/prismaClient.js";
import withHandler from "#shared/utils/withHandler.js";
import { getNamespace } from "#shared/socket.js";
import { sendPushNotificationToUser } from "#shared/utils/pushNotifications.js";

const router = express.Router();

const isNotificationsMutedForUser = ({ chatRoom, userId, mutedSet }) => {
  if (chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
    // Site-wide rooms are muted by default.
    // A row in userMutedChatRoom acts as an explicit opt-in for notifications.
    return !mutedSet.has(userId);
  }

  return mutedSet.has(userId);
};

const SHIFT_NOTIFY_PADDING_MINUTES = 30;

const getShiftNotificationWindow = (now = new Date()) => {
  const paddingMs = SHIFT_NOTIFY_PADDING_MINUTES * 60 * 1000;

  return {
    startsBefore: new Date(now.getTime() + paddingMs),
    endsAfter: new Date(now.getTime() - paddingMs),
  };
};

const emitToThreadParticipants = async ({
  chatNamespace,
  chatRoom,
  threadId,
  event,
  payload,
  excludeUserId = null,
  additionalRoomIds = [],
}) => {
  const roomIds = new Set([
    threadId,
    ...(chatRoom.participants || []).map((participant) => participant.id),
    ...(additionalRoomIds || []),
  ]);

  if (excludeUserId) {
    roomIds.delete(excludeUserId);
  }

  let emitter = chatNamespace;
  [...roomIds].filter(Boolean).forEach((roomId) => {
    emitter = emitter.to(roomId);
  });

  emitter.emit(event, payload);
};

const addCurrentUserPinState = (chat, userId) => {
  const taggedUsers = Array.isArray(chat?.taggedUsers) ? chat.taggedUsers : [];
  const isTaggedForCurrentUser = taggedUsers.some((tag) => tag.userId === userId);

  return {
    ...chat,
    isPinnedForCurrentUser: Boolean(chat?.isPinned || isTaggedForCurrentUser),
  };
};

const extractMentionedUsernames = (content = "") => {
  const matches = String(content).matchAll(/(^|[\s([{:;,])@([A-Za-z0-9_][A-Za-z0-9_.-]{0,31})\b/g);
  return [
    ...new Set(
      [...matches]
        .map((match) => match[2])
        .filter(Boolean)
        .map((username) => username.toLowerCase())
    ),
  ];
};

const findMentionedUsers = async ({ content, chatRoom, organizationId, senderId = null }) => {
  const mentionedUsernames = extractMentionedUsernames(content);
  if (mentionedUsernames.length === 0) return [];

  let addressableUsers = [];
  if (chatRoom.isPrivate) {
    addressableUsers = chatRoom.participants || [];
  } else if (chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
    addressableUsers = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: { active: true },
      select: { id: true, username: true },
    });
  } else {
    addressableUsers = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: { organizationId: chatRoom.organizationId || organizationId, active: true },
      select: { id: true, username: true },
    });
  }

  const mentionedSet = new Set(mentionedUsernames);
  const usersById = new Map();
  const mentionsAll = mentionedSet.has("all");
  addressableUsers.forEach((user) => {
    if (!user?.id || user.id === senderId) return;

    const username = typeof user.username === "string" ? user.username.toLowerCase() : "";
    if (mentionsAll || (username && mentionedSet.has(username))) {
      usersById.set(user.id, { id: user.id, username: user.username });
    }
  });

  return [...usersById.values()];
};

const pushNotifyParticipants = async ({
  chatRoom,
  thread,
  chat,
  excludeUserId = null,
}) => {
  const muted = await prisma.userMutedChatRoom.findMany({
    where: { chatRoomId: chatRoom.id },
    select: { userId: true },
  });
  const mutedSet = new Set(muted.map((m) => m.userId));

  let recipients = [];
  if (chatRoom.isPrivate) {
    recipients = chatRoom.participants || [];
  } else if (chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
    recipients = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: { active: true },
      select: { id: true },
    });
  } else {
    recipients = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: { organizationId: chatRoom.organizationId },
      select: { id: true },
    });
  }

  const url = `/chat?chatRoomId=${encodeURIComponent(chatRoom.id)}&threadId=${encodeURIComponent(thread.id)}&messageId=${encodeURIComponent(chat.id)}`;
  const title = chatRoom.name;
  const taggedUserIds = new Set(
    (Array.isArray(chat.taggedUsers) ? chat.taggedUsers : []).map((tag) => tag.userId)
  );
  let shiftActiveUserIds = null;

  if (chatRoom.shiftNotify && chatRoom.organizationId !== null && recipients.length > 0) {
    const { startsBefore, endsAfter } = getShiftNotificationWindow();
    const activeShifts = await prisma.shift.findMany({
      where: {
        employeeId: { in: recipients.map((recipient) => recipient.id) },
        startTime: { lt: startsBefore },
        endTime: { gt: endsAfter },
      },
      select: { employeeId: true },
      distinct: ["employeeId"],
    });

    shiftActiveUserIds = new Set(activeShifts.map((shift) => shift.employeeId));
  }

  for (const recipient of recipients) {
    if (excludeUserId && recipient.id === excludeUserId) continue;

    const isTagged = taggedUserIds.has(recipient.id);

    if (!isTagged && chatRoom.shiftNotify && chatRoom.organizationId !== null && !shiftActiveUserIds?.has(recipient.id)) {
      continue;
    }

    const isMuted = isNotificationsMutedForUser({
      chatRoom,
      userId: recipient.id,
      mutedSet,
    });

    if (!isTagged && isMuted) continue;

    const contentPreview = chat.content?.trim()
      ? chat.content.trim().replace(/\s+/g, " ").slice(0, 160)
      : "";
    const threadLabel = thread.title && thread.title !== chatRoom.name ? ` · ${thread.title}` : "";
    const body = isTagged
      ? `${chat.sender.username} mentioned you${threadLabel}: ${contentPreview || "Open chat to view the message."}`
      : contentPreview
        ? `${chat.sender.username}: ${contentPreview}`
        : `${chat.sender.username} sent a message${threadLabel}.`;

    const payload = {
      title: isTagged ? `Mention in ${chatRoom.name}` : `${title}${threadLabel}`,
      body,
      chatId: chat.id,
      chatRoomId: chatRoom.id,
      threadId: thread.id,
      messageId: chat.id,
      sender: chat.sender.username,
      senderName: chat.sender.username,
      roomName: chatRoom.name,
      chatRoomName: chatRoom.name,
      threadTitle: thread.title,
      url,
      targetUrl: url,
      type: "CHAT",
      category: "WORKSMRT_CHAT",
      channelId: isTagged ? "urgent" : "chat",
      isMention: isTagged,
      isHighPriority: isTagged,
      priority: isTagged ? "high" : "normal",
    };

    await sendPushNotificationToUser(recipient.id, payload).catch(() => {});
  }
};

const createChat = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatRoomId, threadId, content } = req.body;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  if (!chatRoomId || !threadId || !content) {
    return res
      .status(400)
      .json({ error: "chatRoomId, threadId, and content are required." });
  }

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatRoomId },
      include: { participants: true },
    });

    if (!chatRoom) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chatroom not found." });
    }

    if (
      chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
      chatRoom.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chatroom." });
    }

    if (
      chatRoom.isPrivate &&
      !chatRoom.participants.some((participant) => participant.id === userId)
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chatroom." });
    }

    const thread = await prisma.thread.findUnique({
      where: { id: threadId },
    });
    if (!thread || thread.chatRoomId !== chatRoomId) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid thread ID." });
    }

    const taggedUsers = await findMentionedUsers({ content, chatRoom, organizationId, senderId: userId });

    const newChat = await prisma.chat.create({
      data: {
        content,
        sender: { connect: { id: userId } },
        chatRoom: { connect: { id: chatRoomId } },
        thread: { connect: { id: threadId } },
        ...(taggedUsers.length > 0
          ? {
              taggedUsers: {
                create: taggedUsers.map((taggedUser) => ({
                  user: { connect: { id: taggedUser.id } },
                })),
              },
            }
          : {}),
      },
      include: {
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true, phoneNumber: true } },
        chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true, organizationId: true } },
        thread: { select: { id: true, title: true, chatRoomId: true } },
        taggedUsers: {
          select: {
            userId: true,
            user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
          },
        },
      },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");

    await emitToThreadParticipants({
      chatNamespace,
      chatRoom,
      threadId,
      event: "newChat",
      payload: newChat,
      excludeUserId: null,
      additionalRoomIds: [userId],
    });

    await pushNotifyParticipants({
      chatRoom,
      thread,
      chat: newChat,
      excludeUserId: userId,
    });

    res.status(201).json({ chat: newChat });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Create Chat Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const getChats = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatRoomId, threadId } = req.query;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  if (!chatRoomId || !threadId) {
    return res
      .status(400)
      .json({ error: "chatRoomId and threadId are required." });
  }

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatRoomId },
      include: { participants: true },
    });

    if (!chatRoom) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chatroom not found." });
    }

    if (
      chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
      chatRoom.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chatroom." });
    }

    if (
      chatRoom.isPrivate &&
      !chatRoom.participants.some((participant) => participant.id === userId)
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({
        error: "Access denied to this private chatroom.",
      });
    }

    const thread = await prisma.thread.findUnique({
      where: { id: threadId },
    });
    if (!thread || thread.chatRoomId !== chatRoomId) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid thread ID." });
    }

    const chats = await prisma.chat.findMany({
      where: { threadId },
      include: {
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true, phoneNumber: true } },
        attachments: true,
        thread: { select: { id: true, title: true, chatRoomId: true } },
        chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
        readReceipts: {
          include: { user: { select: { id: true, username: true } } },
        },
        taggedUsers: {
          where: { userId },
          select: {
            userId: true,
            user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
          },
        },
      },
      orderBy: { updatedAt: "asc" },
    });

    const chatsWithPinState = chats
      .map((chat) => addCurrentUserPinState(chat, userId))
      .sort((a, b) => {
        if (a.isPinnedForCurrentUser !== b.isPinnedForCurrentUser) {
          return a.isPinnedForCurrentUser ? -1 : 1;
        }
        return new Date(a.updatedAt) - new Date(b.updatedAt);
      });

    res.status(200).json({ chats: chatsWithPinState });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Get Chats Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const markChatAsRead = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId } = req.params;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  try {
    const chat = await prisma.chat.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatId },
      include: {
        thread: { include: { chatRoom: { include: { participants: true } } } },
      },
    });
    if (!chat) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
    }

    const room = chat.thread.chatRoom;

    if (
      room.organizationId !== null &&
      room.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chat." });
    }

    if (room.isPrivate && !room.participants.some((p) => p.id === userId)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chat." });
    }

    const readReceipt = await prisma.chatReadReceipt.upsert({
      where: { chatId_userId: { chatId, userId } },
      update: { readAt: new Date() },
      create: { chatId, userId, readAt: new Date() },
      include: { user: { select: { id: true, username: true } } },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");
    await emitToThreadParticipants({
      chatNamespace,
      chatRoom: room,
      threadId: chat.threadId,
      event: "chatRead",
      payload: { chatId, readReceipt },
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ readReceipt });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("markChatAsRead Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const confirmRead = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId } = req.params;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  try {
    const chat = await prisma.chat.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatId },
      include: {
        thread: { include: { chatRoom: { include: { participants: true } } } },
      },
    });
    if (!chat) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
    }

    const room = chat.thread.chatRoom;

    if (
      room.organizationId !== null &&
      room.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chat." });
    }

    if (room.isPrivate && !room.participants.some((p) => p.id === userId)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chat." });
    }

    if (!chat.requiresConfirmation) {
      return res
        .status(400)
        .json({ error: "Chat does not require explicit confirmation." });
    }

    const readReceipt = await prisma.chatReadReceipt.upsert({
      where: { chatId_userId: { chatId, userId } },
      update: { readAt: new Date(), confirmedAt: new Date() },
      create: { chatId, userId, readAt: new Date(), confirmedAt: new Date() },
      include: { user: { select: { id: true, username: true } } },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");
    await emitToThreadParticipants({
      chatNamespace,
      chatRoom: room,
      threadId: chat.threadId,
      event: "chatRead",
      payload: { chatId, readReceipt },
    });

    return res.status(200).json({ readReceipt });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("confirmRead Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const markChatAsImportant = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId } = req.params;
  const { isImportant, expiresAt } = req.body;

  if (req.user.role !== "ADMIN") {
    return res
      .status(403)
      .json({ error: "You do not have permission to mark chats as important." });
  }

  try {
    const chat = await prisma.chat.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatId },
      include: {
        thread: { include: { chatRoom: { include: { participants: true } } } },
      },
    });

    if (!chat) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
    }

    const chatRoom = chat.thread.chatRoom;
    if (
      chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
      chatRoom.organizationId !== req.user.organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chat." });
    }

    const updatedChat = await prisma.chat.update({
      where: { id: chatId },
      data: {
        isImportant,
        importantExpiresAt: expiresAt ? new Date(expiresAt) : null,
      },
      include: {
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true, phoneNumber: true } },
        thread: { select: { id: true, title: true, chatRoomId: true } },
        chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
      },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");
    await emitToThreadParticipants({
      chatNamespace,
      chatRoom,
      threadId: chat.threadId,
      event: "importantChatSet",
      payload: updatedChat,
    });

    res.status(200).json({ chat: updatedChat });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Mark Chat as Important Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const getActiveImportantChats = async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;
  const now = new Date();

  try {
    const importantChats = await prisma.chat.findMany({
      where: {
        isImportant: true,
        thread: {
          chatRoom: {
            AND: [
              { organizationId: organizationId },
              { participants: { some: { id: userId } } },
            ],
          },
        },
        OR: [{ importantExpiresAt: null }, { importantExpiresAt: { gt: now } }],
        dismissedBy: {
          none: { userId },
        },
      },
      include: {
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true, phoneNumber: true } },
        chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
        thread: { select: { id: true, title: true, chatRoomId: true } },
      },
      orderBy: { updatedAt: "desc" },
    });

    res.status(200).json({ importantChats });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Get Active Important Chats Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const confirmImportantChat = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId } = req.params;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  try {
    const chat = await prisma.chat.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatId },
      include: {
        thread: {
          include: {
            chatRoom: {
              include: { participants: { select: { id: true } } },
            },
          },
        },
      },
    });

    if (!chat || !chat.isImportant) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Important chat not found." });
    }

    const room = chat.thread.chatRoom;

    const inOrgScope = room.organizationId === organizationId;
    const allowedByPrivacy = room.participants.some((p) => p.id === userId);

    if (!inOrgScope || !allowedByPrivacy) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chat." });
    }

    await prisma.$transaction([
      prisma.userDismissedChat.upsert({
        where: { userId_chatId: { userId, chatId } },
        update: {},
        create: { userId, chatId },
      }),
      prisma.chatReadReceipt.upsert({
        where: { chatId_userId: { chatId, userId } },
        update: { popupConfirmedAt: new Date() },
        create: { chatId, userId, popupConfirmedAt: new Date() },
      }),
    ]);

    return res
      .status(200)
      .json({ message: "Important chat confirmed and dismissed." });
  } catch (error) {
    if (error.code === "P2003") {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
    }
    console.error("Confirm Important Chat Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const pinChat = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId } = req.params;
  const { isPinned } = req.body;

  if (req.user.role !== "ADMIN") {
    return res
      .status(403)
      .json({ error: "You do not have permission to pin messages." });
  }

  if (typeof isPinned !== "boolean") {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "isPinned must be a boolean value." });
  }

  try {
    const chat = await prisma.chat.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatId },
      include: {
        thread: { include: { chatRoom: { include: { participants: true } } } },
      },
    });

    if (!chat) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
    }

    const chatRoom = chat.thread.chatRoom;
    if (
      chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
      chatRoom.organizationId !== req.user.organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this chat." });
    }

    const updatedChat = await prisma.chat.update({
      where: { id: chatId },
      data: { isPinned },
      include: {
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true, phoneNumber: true } },
        attachments: true,
        thread: { select: { id: true, title: true, chatRoomId: true } },
        chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
        readReceipts: {
          include: { user: { select: { id: true, username: true } } },
        },
        taggedUsers: {
          select: {
            userId: true,
            user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
          },
        },
      },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");
    await emitToThreadParticipants({
      chatNamespace,
      chatRoom,
      threadId: chat.threadId,
      event: "chatUpdated",
      payload: addCurrentUserPinState(updatedChat, req.user.id || req.user.userId),
    });

    res.status(200).json({ chat: addCurrentUserPinState(updatedChat, req.user.id || req.user.userId) });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Pin Chat Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const getPinnedChats = async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  try {
    const pinnedChats = await prisma.chat.findMany({
      where: {
        OR: [
          { isPinned: true },
          { taggedUsers: { some: { userId } } },
        ],
        thread: {
          chatRoom: {
            organizationId,
            OR: [
              { isPrivate: false },
              { participants: { some: { id: userId } } },
            ],
          },
        },
        dismissedBy: {
          none: { userId },
        },
      },
      include: {
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true, phoneNumber: true } },
        chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
        thread: { select: { id: true, title: true, chatRoomId: true } },
        taggedUsers: {
          where: { userId },
          select: {
            userId: true,
            user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
          },
        },
      },
      orderBy: { updatedAt: "desc" },
    });
    res.status(200).json({
      pinnedChats: pinnedChats.map((chat) => addCurrentUserPinState(chat, userId)),
    });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Get Pinned Chats Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const deleteChat = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId } = req.params;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const userRole = req.user.role;

  try {
    const chat = await prisma.chat.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatId },
      include: {
        chatRoom: { include: { participants: true } },
        thread: true,
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true, phoneNumber: true } },
      },
    });

    if (!chat) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
    }

    if (chat.senderId !== userId && userRole !== "ADMIN") {
      return res
        .status(403)
        .json({ error: "You do not have permission to delete this message." });
    }

    await prisma.chat.delete({
      where: { id: chatId },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");
    await emitToThreadParticipants({
      chatNamespace,
      chatRoom: chat.chatRoom,
      threadId: chat.threadId,
      event: "chatDeleted",
      payload: { chatId, threadId: chat.threadId },
    });

    res.status(200).json({ message: "Chat deleted successfully." });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Delete Chat Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

router.post(
  "/",
  withHandler({
    handler: createChat,
    allowedMethods: ["POST"],
  })
);

router.get(
  "/",
  withHandler({
    handler: getChats,
    allowedMethods: ["GET"],
  })
);

router.delete(
  "/:chatId",
  withHandler({
    handler: deleteChat,
    allowedMethods: ["DELETE"],
  })
);

router.put(
  "/:chatId/read",
  withHandler({
    handler: markChatAsRead,
    allowedMethods: ["PUT"],
  })
);

router.put(
  "/:chatId/confirm",
  withHandler({
    handler: confirmRead,
    allowedMethods: ["PUT"],
  })
);

router.put(
  "/:chatId/mark-important",
  withHandler({
    handler: markChatAsImportant,
    allowedMethods: ["PUT"],
  })
);

router.put(
  "/:chatId/pin",
  withHandler({
    handler: pinChat,
    allowedMethods: ["PUT"],
  })
);

router.get(
  "/pinned",
  withHandler({
    handler: getPinnedChats,
    allowedMethods: ["GET"],
  })
);

router.get(
  "/important/active",
  withHandler({
    handler: getActiveImportantChats,
    allowedMethods: ["GET"],
  })
);

router.put(
  "/:chatId/confirm-important",
  withHandler({
    handler: confirmImportantChat,
    allowedMethods: ["PUT"],
  })
);

export default router;
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/conversations.js
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import { getIO } from '#shared/socket.js'; // Ensure getIO is exported correctly

const router = express.Router();

const createConversation = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatRoomId, title } = req.body;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;

  if (!chatRoomId || !title) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'chatRoomId and title are required.' });
  }

  try {
    // Verify user participation
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatRoomId },
      include: { participants: true },
    });

    if (
      !chatRoom ||
      !chatRoom.participants.some(participant => participant.id === userId)
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied to this chatroom.' });
    }

    const newConversation = await prisma.conversation.create({
      data: {
        title,
        chatRoom: { connect: { id: chatRoomId } },
      },
    });

    // Emit to chat room namespace that a new conversation has been created
    const io = getIO();
    io.to(chatRoomId).emit('newConversation', newConversation);

    res.status(201).json({ conversation: newConversation });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Create Conversation Error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

const getConversations = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatRoomId } = req.query;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;

  if (!chatRoomId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'chatRoomId is required.' });
  }

  try {
    // Verify user participation
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatRoomId },
      include: { participants: true },
    });

    if (
      !chatRoom ||
      !chatRoom.participants.some(participant => participant.id === userId)
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied to this chatroom.' });
    }

    const conversations = await prisma.conversation.findMany({
      where: { chatRoomId },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });

    res.status(200).json({ conversations });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Get Conversations Error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

router.post('/', createConversation);
router.get('/', getConversations);

export default router;

```

FILE: server/src/routes/api/chat/gifs.js

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/gifs.js
import express from "express";
import withHandler from "#shared/utils/withHandler.js";

const router = express.Router();

const searchGifs = async (req, res) => {
  const { q, limit = 12, offset = 0 } = req.query;

  if (!q) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Search query 'q' is required." });
  }

  const apiKey = process.env.GIPHY_API_KEY || process.env.TENOR_API_KEY;

  if (!apiKey) {
    return res.status(500).json({
      error: "GIF API key not configured. Set GIPHY_API_KEY or TENOR_API_KEY in environment.",
    });
  }

  try {
    if (process.env.GIPHY_API_KEY) {
      const giphyRes = await fetch(
        `https://api.giphy.com/v1/gifs/search?api_key=${encodeURIComponent(apiKey)}&q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}&limit=${limit}&offset=${offset}&rating=g&lang=en`,
      );

      if (!giphyRes.ok) {
        throw new Error(`Giphy API error: ${giphyRes.status}`);
      }

      const data = await giphyRes.json();

      const gifs = (data.data || []).map((gif) => ({
        id: gif.id,
        url: gif.images.original.url,
        previewUrl: gif.images.fixed_height_downsampled?.url || gif.images.preview_gif?.url,
        width: gif.images.original.width,
        height: gif.images.original.height,
        title: gif.title || "",
        provider: "giphy",
        attribution: "Powered by GIPHY",
      }));

      return res.status(200).json({ gifs, pagination: data.pagination });
    }

    if (process.env.TENOR_API_KEY) {
      const tenorRes = await fetch(
        `https://tenor.googleapis.com/v2/search?key=${encodeURIComponent(apiKey)}&q=${encodeURIComponent(q)}&limit=${limit}&pos=${offset}`,
      );

      if (!tenorRes.ok) {
        throw new Error(`Tenor API error: ${tenorRes.status}`);
      }

      const data = await tenorRes.json();

      const gifs = (data.results || []).map((gif) => {
        const media = gif.media_formats?.gif || gif.media_formats?.tinygif || {};
        const preview = gif.media_formats?.tinygif || gif.media_formats?.gif || {};
        return {
          id: gif.id,
          url: media.url || "",
          previewUrl: preview.url || "",
          width: media.dimensions?.[0] || gif.width,
          height: media.dimensions?.[1] || gif.height,
          title: gif.title || gif.content_description || "",
          provider: "tenor",
          attribution: "Powered by Tenor",
        };
      });

      return res.status(200).json({ gifs, pagination: { total_count: data.total_count || 0, count: gifs.length } });
    }
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("GIF Search Error:", error);
    return res.status(502).json({ error: "Failed to search GIFs." });
  }
};

router.get("/search", withHandler({ handler: searchGifs, allowedMethods: ["GET"] }));

export default router;
```

FILE: server/src/routes/api/chat/reactions.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/reactions.js
import express from "express";
import prisma from "#shared/database/prismaClient.js";
import withHandler from "#shared/utils/withHandler.js";
import { getNamespace } from "#shared/socket.js";

const router = express.Router();

const addReaction = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId, emoji } = req.body;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;

  if (!chatId || !emoji) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "chatId and emoji are required." });
  }

  if (typeof emoji !== "string" || [...emoji].length > 4) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "Invalid emoji." });
  }

  try {
    const chat = await prisma.chat.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatId },
      include: {
        thread: { include: { chatRoom: { include: { participants: true } } } },
      },
    });

    if (!chat) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
    }

    const room = chat.thread.chatRoom;
    if (
      room.organizationId !== null &&
      room.organizationId !== req.user.organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied." });
    }

    if (room.isPrivate && !room.participants.some((p) => p.id === userId)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied." });
    }

    const reaction = await prisma.chatReaction.upsert({
      where: { chatId_userId_emoji: { chatId, userId, emoji } },
      update: {},
      create: { chatId, userId, emoji },
      include: {
        user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
      },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");
    chatNamespace.to(chat.threadId).to(userId).emit("reactionAdded", {
      chatId,
      reaction: {
        ...reaction,
        chatId,
        userId,
        emoji,
      },
    });

    res.status(201).json({ reaction });
  } catch (error) {
    if (error.code === "P2002") {
      return res.status(409).json({ error: "Reaction already exists." });
    }
    console.error("Add Reaction Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const removeReaction = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId, emoji } = req.params;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;

  if (!chatId || !emoji) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "chatId and emoji are required." });
  }

  try {
    const decodedEmoji = decodeURIComponent(emoji);

    const chat = await prisma.chat.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatId },
      include: {
        thread: { include: { chatRoom: { include: { participants: true } } } },
      },
    });

    if (!chat) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
    }

    const room = chat.thread.chatRoom;
    if (
      room.organizationId !== null &&
      room.organizationId !== req.user.organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied." });
    }

    if (room.isPrivate && !room.participants.some((p) => p.id === userId)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied." });
    }

    await prisma.chatReaction.delete({
      where: { chatId_userId_emoji: { chatId, userId, emoji: decodedEmoji } },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");
    chatNamespace.to(chat.threadId).to(userId).emit("reactionRemoved", {
      chatId,
      userId,
      emoji: decodedEmoji,
    });

    res.status(200).json({ message: "Reaction removed." });
  } catch (error) {
    if (error.code === "P2025") {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Reaction not found." });
    }
    console.error("Remove Reaction Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

const getReactions = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatId } = req.params;

  if (!chatId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "chatId is required." });
  }

  try {
    const reactions = await prisma.chatReaction.findMany({
      where: { chatId },
      include: {
        user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
      },
    });

    res.status(200).json({ reactions });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Get Reactions Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

router.post("/", withHandler({ handler: addReaction, allowedMethods: ["POST"] }));
router.delete("/:chatId/:emoji", withHandler({ handler: removeReaction, allowedMethods: ["DELETE"] }));
router.get("/:chatId", withHandler({ handler: getReactions, allowedMethods: ["GET"] }));

export default router;
```

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/recent.js
// server/src/routes/api/chat/recent.js
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';

const router = express.Router();

const getRecentChats = async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  try {
    const recentChats = await prisma.chat.findMany({
      where: {
        chatRoom: {
          organizationId,
          // Allow public rooms or private rooms where the user is a participant
          OR: [
            { isPrivate: false },
            { isPrivate: true, participants: { some: { id: userId } } }
          ]
        }
      },
      include: {
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
        chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
        thread: { select: { id: true, title: true } },
        attachments: true,
      },
      orderBy: { updatedAt: 'desc' },
      take: 20,
    });

    res.status(200).json({ recentChats });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Get Recent Chats Error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
};

router.get('/', withHandler({
  handler: getRecentChats,
  allowedMethods: ['GET']
}));

export default router;
```
