----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: server/src/routes/api/chat/sendChat.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/sendChat.js
import express from "express";
import multer from "multer";
import path from "path";
import { v4 as uuidv4 } from "uuid";
import prisma from "#shared/database/prismaClient.js";
import { errorHandler } from "#middleware/errorHandler.js";
import authenticate from "#middleware/auth.js";
import fs from "fs-extra";
import { getIO } from "#shared/socket.js";
import { sendPushNotificationToUser } from "#shared/utils/pushNotifications.js";
import { extractRequestContext, logAndReportError } from "../../../utils/logError.js";

const router = express.Router();

const isNotificationsMutedForUser = ({ room, userId, mutedUserIds }) => {
  if (room.organizationId === null) {
    // Site-wide rooms are muted by default.
    // A record in userMutedChatRoom acts as an explicit opt-in for notifications.
    return !mutedUserIds.has(userId);
  }

  return mutedUserIds.has(userId);
};

const SHIFT_NOTIFY_PADDING_MINUTES = 30;

const getShiftNotificationWindow = (now = new Date()) => {
  const paddingMs = SHIFT_NOTIFY_PADDING_MINUTES * 60 * 1000;

  return {
    startsBefore: new Date(now.getTime() + paddingMs),
    endsAfter: new Date(now.getTime() - paddingMs),
  };
};

const emitToRooms = ({ namespace, roomIds, event, payload }) => {
  const uniqueRoomIds = [...new Set((roomIds || []).filter(Boolean))];
  if (uniqueRoomIds.length === 0) return;

  let emitter = namespace;
  uniqueRoomIds.forEach((roomId) => {
    emitter = emitter.to(roomId);
  });

  emitter.emit(event, payload);
};

const extractMentionedUsernames = (content = "") => {
  const matches = String(content).matchAll(/(^|[\s([{:;,])@([A-Za-z0-9_][A-Za-z0-9_.-]{0,31})\b/g);
  return [
    ...new Set(
      [...matches]
        .map((match) => match[2])
        .filter(Boolean)
        .map((username) => username.toLowerCase())
    ),
  ];
};

const findMentionedUsers = async ({ content, room, organizationId, senderId = null }) => {
  const mentionedUsernames = extractMentionedUsernames(content);

  if (mentionedUsernames.length === 0) {
    return [];
  }

  let addressableUsers = [];
  if (room.isPrivate) {
    addressableUsers = room.participants || [];
  } else if (room.organizationId === null) {
    addressableUsers = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: { active: true },
      select: { id: true, username: true },
    });
  } else {
    addressableUsers = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: { organizationId: room.organizationId || organizationId, active: true },
      select: { id: true, username: true },
    });
  }

  const mentionedSet = new Set(mentionedUsernames);
  const uniqueById = new Map();
  const mentionsAll = mentionedSet.has("all");

  addressableUsers.forEach((user) => {
    if (!user?.id || user.id === senderId) return;

    const username = typeof user.username === "string" ? user.username.toLowerCase() : "";
    if (mentionsAll || (username && mentionedSet.has(username))) {
      uniqueById.set(user.id, { id: user.id, username: user.username });
    }
  });

  return [...uniqueById.values()];
};

const storage = multer.diskStorage({
  destination: async (req, file, cb) => {
    let organizationIdForPath;
    const { threadId } = req.body;

    if (threadId) {
      try {
        const thread = await prisma.thread.findUnique({
          where: { id: threadId },
          include: { chatRoom: true },
        });

        if (thread && thread.chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
          organizationIdForPath = "global";
        } else {
          organizationIdForPath = req.user.organizationId;
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error("Error finding thread for upload destination:", e);
        organizationIdForPath = req.user.organizationId;
      }
    } else {
      organizationIdForPath = req.user.organizationId;
    }

    const uploadDir = path.join(
      process.cwd(),
      "uploads",
      organizationIdForPath,
      "chats",
      "files"
    );

    try {
      await fs.ensureDir(uploadDir);
      cb(null, uploadDir);
    } catch (err) {
      console.error("Error creating upload directory:", err);
      cb(err, uploadDir);
    }
  },
  filename: (req, file, cb) => {
    const uniqueName = `${uuidv4()}${path.extname(file.originalname)}`;
    cb(null, uniqueName);
  },
});

const upload = multer({
  storage,
  fileFilter: (req, file, cb) => {
    const allowedTypes = [
      "image/jpeg",
      "image/png",
      "image/gif",
      "video/mp4",
      "video/mpeg",
    ];
    if (allowedTypes.includes(file.mimetype)) {
      cb(null, true);
    } else {
      cb(
        new Error(
          "Invalid file type. Only JPEG, PNG, GIF, MP4, and MPEG are allowed."
        )
      );
    }
  },
  limits: { fileSize: 10 * 1024 * 1024 },
});

const sendChatHandler = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { threadId, content, isImportant, importantExpiresAt } = req.body;
    const files = req.files;
    const authUser = req.user || {};
    const userId = authUser.id || authUser.userId || null;
    const organizationId = authUser.organizationId || null;

    if (!userId) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: "Unauthorized: missing user context." });
    }

    if (!threadId) {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: "threadId is required." });
    }

    const thread = await prisma.thread.findUnique({
      where: { id: threadId },
      include: {
        chatRoom: {
          include: {
            participants: true,
            mutedBy: {
              select: { userId: true },
            },
          },
        },
      },
    });

    if (!thread) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: "Thread not found." });
    }

    const room = thread.chatRoom;

    if (
      room.organizationId !== null &&
      room.organizationId !== organizationId
    ) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: "Access denied to this thread." });
    }

    if (
      room.isPrivate &&
      !room.participants.some((participant) => participant.id === userId)
    ) {
      return res
        .status(403)
        .json({ error: "You are not a participant of this thread." });
    }

    const taggedUsers = await findMentionedUsers({ content, room, organizationId, senderId: userId });

    const isSiteWide = room.organizationId === null;
    const attachmentOrgPath = isSiteWide ? "global" : organizationId;

    const data = {
      content: content || "",
      sender: { connect: { id: userId } },
      chatRoom: { connect: { id: room.id } },
      thread: { connect: { id: threadId } },
      isImportant: isImportant === "true" || isImportant === true,
      importantExpiresAt: importantExpiresAt
        ? new Date(importantExpiresAt)
        : null,
    };

    if (files && files.length > 0) {
      data.attachments = {
        create: files.map((file) => ({
          url: `/uploads/${attachmentOrgPath}/chats/files/${file.filename}`,
          filename: file.originalname,
          mimetype: file.mimetype,
          size: file.size,
        })),
      };
    }

    if (taggedUsers.length > 0) {
      data.taggedUsers = {
        create: taggedUsers.map((taggedUser) => ({
          user: { connect: { id: taggedUser.id } },
        })),
      };
    }

    const chat = await prisma.chat.create({
      data,
      include: {
        sender: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
        attachments: true,
        chatRoom: {
          select: { id: true, name: true, shiftNotify: true },
        },
        thread: { select: { id: true, title: true, chatRoomId: true } },
        taggedUsers: {
          select: {
            userId: true,
            user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
          },
        },
      },
    });

    const chatNamespace = getIO().of("/chat");

    // Deliver to the thread room and the sender's personal room in one union emit,
    // so the sender still gets the event even if their client isn't actively joined
    // to the thread room, without duplicate delivery when both rooms are joined.
    emitToRooms({
      namespace: chatNamespace,
      roomIds: [chat.thread.id, userId],
      event: "newChat",
      payload: chat,
    });

    let recipients = [];
    if (room.isPrivate) {
      recipients = room.participants.filter(
        (participant) => participant.id !== userId
      );
    } else if (isSiteWide) {
      recipients = await prisma.user.findMany({
        where: { active: true, id: { not: userId } },
        select: { id: true },
      });
    } else {
      recipients = await prisma.user.findMany({
        where: {
          organizationId: room.organizationId,
          id: { not: userId },
        },
        select: { id: true },
      });
    }

    const mutedUserIds = new Set(room.mutedBy.map((mute) => mute.userId));
    const taggedUserIds = new Set(taggedUsers.map((u) => u.id));

    let shiftActiveUserIds = null;
    if (room.shiftNotify && !isSiteWide && recipients.length > 0) {
      const { startsBefore, endsAfter } = getShiftNotificationWindow();
      const activeShifts = await prisma.shift.findMany({
        where: {
          employeeId: { in: recipients.map((recipient) => recipient.id) },
          startTime: { lt: startsBefore },
          endTime: { gt: endsAfter },
        },
        select: { employeeId: true },
        distinct: ["employeeId"],
      });

      shiftActiveUserIds = new Set(
        activeShifts.map((shift) => shift.employeeId)
      );
    }

    const backgroundRecipients = recipients.filter((recipient) => {
      const isTagged = taggedUserIds.has(recipient.id);

      if (!isTagged && room.shiftNotify && !isSiteWide && !shiftActiveUserIds?.has(recipient.id)) {
        return false;
      }

      const isMuted = isNotificationsMutedForUser({
        room,
        userId: recipient.id,
        mutedUserIds,
      });

      if (!isTagged && isMuted) {
        return false;
      }

      return true;
    });

    // Live/background events for other users who should receive them.
    backgroundRecipients.forEach((recipient) => {
      chatNamespace.to(recipient.id).emit("newChat", chat);
    });

    for (const recipient of backgroundRecipients) {
      let notificationBody;
      const isTagged = taggedUserIds.has(recipient.id);

      if (isTagged) {
        notificationBody = `${chat.sender.username} mentioned you: ${chat.content || "Open chat to view the message."}`;
      } else if (chat.content) {
        notificationBody = chat.content;
      } else if (chat.attachments && chat.attachments.length > 0) {
        notificationBody = `${chat.sender.username} sent ${chat.attachments.length} attachment(s).`;
      }

      if (!notificationBody || notificationBody.trim() === "") {
        continue;
      }

      const payload = {
        title: isTagged
          ? `High priority mention in ${room.name}`
          : room.name,
        body: notificationBody,
        chatId: chat.id,
        chatRoomId: chat.thread.chatRoomId,
        threadId: chat.thread.id,
        sender: chat.sender.username,
        roomName: room.name,
        threadTitle: chat.thread.title,
        url: `/dash?openChat=true&chatRoomId=${chat.thread.chatRoomId}&threadId=${chat.thread.id}&messageId=${chat.id}`,
        type: "CHAT",
        isMention: isTagged,
        isHighPriority: isTagged,
        priority: isTagged ? "high" : "normal",
      };

      try {
        await sendPushNotificationToUser(recipient.id, payload);
      } catch (err) {
        console.error("Push notification failed:", err);
      }
    }

    res.status(201).json({ chat });
  } catch (error) {
    await logAndReportError("Send Chat Message Error:", error, extractRequestContext(req));
    res
      .status(500)
      .json({ error: "Internal server error while processing chat." });
  }
};

router.post("/", authenticate, upload.array("attachments", 5), sendChatHandler);

router.use(errorHandler);

export default router;

```

----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
FILE: server/src/routes/api/chat/sockets.js
----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/sockets.js
import { getNamespace } from "#shared/socket.js";
import prisma from "#shared/database/prismaClient.js";
import jwt from "jsonwebtoken";
import cookie from "cookie";
import { sendPushNotificationToUser } from "#shared/utils/pushNotifications.js";

const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || "your_jwt_secret_here";

const canAccessChatRoom = ({ chatRoom, user }) => {
  if (!chatRoom || !user) return false;

  if (
    chatRoom.organizationId !== null &&
    chatRoom.organizationId !== user.organizationId
  ) {
    return false;
  }

  if (chatRoom.isPrivate) {
    return chatRoom.participants.some((participant) => participant.id === user.id);
  }

  return true;
};

const isNotificationsMutedForUser = ({ chatRoom, userId, mutedSet }) => {
  if (chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
    // Site-wide rooms are muted by default.
    // A row in userMutedChatRoom acts as an explicit opt-in for notifications.
    return !mutedSet.has(userId);
  }

  return mutedSet.has(userId);
};

const SHIFT_NOTIFY_PADDING_MINUTES = 30;

const getShiftNotificationWindow = (now = new Date()) => {
  const paddingMs = SHIFT_NOTIFY_PADDING_MINUTES * 60 * 1000;

  return {
    startsBefore: new Date(now.getTime() + paddingMs),
    endsAfter: new Date(now.getTime() - paddingMs),
  };
};

const extractMentionedUsernames = (content = "") => {
  const matches = String(content).matchAll(/(^|[\s([{:;,])@([A-Za-z0-9_][A-Za-z0-9_.-]{0,31})\b/g);
  return [
    ...new Set(
      [...matches]
        .map((match) => match[2])
        .filter(Boolean)
        .map((username) => username.toLowerCase())
    ),
  ];
};

const findMentionedUsers = async ({ content, chatRoom, senderId = null }) => {
  const mentionedUsernames = extractMentionedUsernames(content);
  if (mentionedUsernames.length === 0) return [];

  let addressableUsers = [];
  if (chatRoom.isPrivate) {
    addressableUsers = chatRoom.participants || [];
  } else if (chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
    addressableUsers = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: { active: true },
      select: { id: true, username: true },
    });
  } else {
    addressableUsers = await prisma.user.findMany({
      where: { organizationId: chatRoom.organizationId, active: true },
      select: { id: true, username: true },
    });
  }

  const mentionedSet = new Set(mentionedUsernames);
  const uniqueById = new Map();
  const mentionsAll = mentionedSet.has("all");
  addressableUsers.forEach((user) => {
    if (!user?.id || user.id === senderId) return;

    const username = typeof user.username === "string" ? user.username.toLowerCase() : "";
    if (mentionsAll || (username && mentionedSet.has(username))) {
      uniqueById.set(user.id, { id: user.id, username: user.username });
    }
  });

  return [...uniqueById.values()];
};

const setupChatSockets = () => {
  const chatNamespace = getNamespace("/chat");

  chatNamespace.use(async (socket, next) => {
    try {
      const cookies = socket.handshake.headers.cookie;
      if (!cookies) {
        return next(new Error("Authentication error: No cookies sent"));
      }

      const parsedCookies = cookie.parse(cookies);
      const token = parsedCookies.token;

      if (!token) {
        return next(new Error("Authentication error: No token provided"));
      }

      let decoded;
      try {
        decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
      } catch (err) {
        if (err.name === "TokenExpiredError") {
          return next(
            new Error("Authentication error: token expired. Please log in again.")
          );
        }
        return next(new Error("Authentication error: invalid token."));
      }

      const user = await prisma.user.findUnique({
        where: { id: decoded.userId },
        include: { organization: true },
      });

      if (!user) {
        return next(new Error("Authentication error: User not found"));
      }

      socket.user = user;
      socket.organizationId = user.organizationId;

      socket.join(user.id);

      next();
    } catch (error) {
      console.error("Chat Socket.IO auth error:", error);
      next(new Error("Authentication error"));
    }
  });

  chatNamespace.on("connection", (socket) => {
    socket.on("joinThread", async (threadId) => {
      try {
        const thread = await prisma.thread.findUnique({
          where: { id: threadId },
          include: { chatRoom: { include: { participants: true } } },
        });

        if (!thread) {
          socket.emit("error", "Thread not found.");
          return;
        }

        if (!canAccessChatRoom({ chatRoom: thread.chatRoom, user: socket.user })) {
          socket.emit("error", "Access denied to this thread.");
          return;
        }

        socket.join(threadId);
        socket.emit("joinedThread", threadId);
        console.log(`${socket.user.username} joined thread ${threadId}`);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Join Thread Error:", error);
        socket.emit("error", "Failed to join thread.");
      }
    });

    socket.on("createThread", async ({ chatRoomId, title }) => {
      try {
        const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
          where: { id: chatRoomId },
          include: { participants: true },
        });

        if (!chatRoom) {
          socket.emit("error", "Chatroom not found.");
          return;
        }

        if (!canAccessChatRoom({ chatRoom, user: socket.user })) {
          socket.emit("error", "Access denied to this chatroom.");
          return;
        }

        const newThread = await prisma.thread.create({
          data: {
            title,
            chatRoom: { connect: { id: chatRoomId } },
          },
        });

        const recipientIds = new Set([
          socket.user.id,
          ...(chatRoom.participants || []).map((participant) => participant.id),
        ]);

        let emitter = chatNamespace;
        [...recipientIds].forEach((recipientId) => {
          emitter = emitter.to(recipientId);
        });
        emitter.emit("newThread", newThread);

        console.log(
          `New thread "${title}" created and emitted for room ${chatRoomId}`
        );
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Create Thread via Socket Error:", error);
        socket.emit("error", "Failed to create thread.");
      }
    });

    socket.on("sendMessage", async ({ chatRoomId, threadId, content }) => {
      try {
        const userId = socket.user.id;

        if (!chatRoomId || !threadId || !content) {
          socket.emit(
            "error",
            "chatRoomId, threadId, and content are required."
          );
          return;
        }

        const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
          where: { id: chatRoomId },
          include: { participants: true },
        });

        if (!chatRoom || !canAccessChatRoom({ chatRoom, user: socket.user })) {
          socket.emit("error", "Access denied to this chatroom.");
          return;
        }

        const thread = await prisma.thread.findUnique({
          where: { id: threadId },
        });

        if (!thread || thread.chatRoomId !== chatRoomId) {
          socket.emit("error", "Invalid thread ID.");
          return;
        }

        const taggedUsers = await findMentionedUsers({ content, chatRoom, senderId: userId });

        const newChat = await prisma.chat.create({
          data: {
            content,
            sender: { connect: { id: userId } },
            chatRoom: { connect: { id: chatRoomId } },
            thread: { connect: { id: threadId } },
            ...(taggedUsers.length > 0
              ? {
                  taggedUsers: {
                    create: taggedUsers.map((taggedUser) => ({
                      user: { connect: { id: taggedUser.id } },
                    })),
                  },
                }
              : {}),
          },
          include: {
            sender: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
            chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true, organizationId: true } },
            thread: { select: { id: true, title: true, chatRoomId: true } },
            taggedUsers: {
              select: {
                userId: true,
                user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
              },
            },
          },
        });

        // Union emit to the thread room plus the sender's personal room
        // so the sender always sees their own message.
        chatNamespace.to(threadId).to(userId).emit("newChat", newChat);

        // Also emit to other explicit participants' personal rooms.
        for (const participant of chatRoom.participants) {
          if (participant.id === userId) continue;
          chatNamespace.to(participant.id).emit("newChat", newChat);
        }

        const muted = await prisma.userMutedChatRoom.findMany({
          where: { chatRoomId },
          select: { userId: true },
        });
        const mutedSet = new Set(muted.map((m) => m.userId));

        let recipients = [];
        if (chatRoom.isPrivate) {
          recipients = chatRoom.participants || [];
        } else if (chatRoom.organizationId === null) {
          recipients = await prisma.user.findMany({
            where: { active: true },
            select: { id: true },
          });
        } else {
          recipients = await prisma.user.findMany({
            where: { organizationId: chatRoom.organizationId },
            select: { id: true },
          });
        }

        const url = `/dash?openChat=true&chatRoomId=${chatRoomId}&threadId=${threadId}`;
        const title = chatRoom.name;
        const taggedUserIds = new Set(taggedUsers.map((taggedUser) => taggedUser.id));
        let shiftActiveUserIds = null;

        if (chatRoom.shiftNotify && chatRoom.organizationId !== null && recipients.length > 0) {
          const { startsBefore, endsAfter } = getShiftNotificationWindow();
          const activeShifts = await prisma.shift.findMany({
            where: {
              employeeId: { in: recipients.map((recipient) => recipient.id) },
              startTime: { lt: startsBefore },
              endTime: { gt: endsAfter },
            },
            select: { employeeId: true },
            distinct: ["employeeId"],
          });

          shiftActiveUserIds = new Set(activeShifts.map((shift) => shift.employeeId));
        }

        for (const recipient of recipients) {
          if (recipient.id === userId) continue;

          const isTagged = taggedUserIds.has(recipient.id);

          if (!isTagged && chatRoom.shiftNotify && chatRoom.organizationId !== null && !shiftActiveUserIds?.has(recipient.id)) {
            continue;
          }

          const isMuted = isNotificationsMutedForUser({
            chatRoom,
            userId: recipient.id,
            mutedSet,
          });

          if (!isTagged && isMuted) continue;

          const payload = {
            title: isTagged ? `High priority mention in ${chatRoom.name}` : title,
            body: isTagged
              ? `${socket.user.username} mentioned you: ${content.slice(0, 120) || "Open chat to view the message."}`
              : `${socket.user.username}: ${content.slice(0, 120)}`,
            chatId: newChat.id,
            chatRoomId,
            threadId,
            sender: socket.user.username,
            roomName: chatRoom.name,
            threadTitle: thread.title,
            url: `${url}&messageId=${newChat.id}`,
            type: "CHAT",
            isMention: isTagged,
            isHighPriority: isTagged,
            priority: isTagged ? "high" : "normal",
          };

          await sendPushNotificationToUser(recipient.id, payload).catch(() => {});
        }

        console.log(
          `New chat from ${socket.user.username} emitted to thread ${threadId} and personal recipients`
        );
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Send Chat Error:", error);
        socket.emit("error", "Internal server error.");
      }
    });

    socket.on("leaveThread", (threadId) => {
      socket.leave(threadId);
      socket.emit("leftThread", threadId);
    });

    socket.on("chatRoomUpdated", (updatedChatRoom) => {
    });

    socket.on("disconnect", () => {
    });
  });
};

export default setupChatSockets;

```

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/threads.js
// server/src/routes/api/chat/threads.js

import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';
import { getIO } from '#shared/socket.js'; 

const router = express.Router();

const createThread = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatRoomId, title } = req.body;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  if (!chatRoomId || !title) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'chatRoomId and title are required.' });
  }

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatRoomId },
      include: { participants: true },
    });

    // --- MODIFICATION START ---
    // Allow access if the room is site-wide or belongs to the user's org.
    if (!chatRoom || (chatRoom.organizationId !== null && chatRoom.organizationId !== organizationId)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied to this chatroom.' });
    }
    // --- MODIFICATION END ---

    if (chatRoom.isPrivate && !chatRoom.participants.some(participant => participant.id === userId)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied to this chatroom.' });
    }

    const newThread = await prisma.thread.create({
      data: {
        title,
        chatRoom: { connect: { id: chatRoomId } },
      },
    });

    const io = getIO();
    io.to(chatRoomId).emit('newThread', newThread);

    res.status(201).json({ thread: newThread });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Create Thread Error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

const getThreads = async (req, res) => {
  const { chatRoomId } = req.query;
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;

  if (!chatRoomId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: 'chatRoomId is required.' });
  }

  try {
    const chatRoom = await prisma.chatRoom.findUnique({
      where: { id: chatRoomId },
      include: { participants: true },
    });

    // --- MODIFICATION START ---
    // Allow access if the room is site-wide or belongs to the user's org.
    if (!chatRoom || (chatRoom.organizationId !== null && chatRoom.organizationId !== organizationId)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied to this chatroom.' });
    }
    // --- MODIFICATION END ---

    if (chatRoom.isPrivate && !chatRoom.participants.some(participant => participant.id === userId)) {
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Access denied to this chatroom.' });
    }

    const threads = await prisma.thread.findMany({
      where: { chatRoomId },
      orderBy: { createdAt: 'desc' },
    });

    res.status(200).json({ threads });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error('Get Threads Error:', error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Internal server error.' });
  }
};

router.post('/', withHandler({
  handler: createThread,
  allowedMethods: ['POST'],
}));

router.get('/', withHandler({
  handler: getThreads,
  allowedMethods: ['GET'],
}));

export default router;
```

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/unread.js
//--- File: server/src/routes/api/chat/unread.js ---
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';

const router = express.Router();

router.get('/', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;
  try {
    const unreadCounts = await prisma.chat.groupBy({
      by: ['chatRoomId'],
      where: {
        chatRoom: { organizationId },
        readReceipts: {
          none: { userId },
        },
      },
      _count: { id: true },
    });
    res.status(200).json({ unreadCounts });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Unread counts error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
});

export default router;

```

// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/unreadThreads.js
//--- File: server/src/routes/api/chat/unreadThreads.js ---
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import authenticate from '#middleware/auth.js';

const router = express.Router();

router.get('/', authenticate, async (req, res) => {
  const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
  const { chatRoomId } = req.query;
  if (!chatRoomId) {
    return res.status(400).json({ error: "chatRoomId is required." });
  }
  try {
    const unreadCounts = await prisma.chat.groupBy({
      by: ['threadId'],
      where: {
        chatRoomId,
        readReceipts: {
          none: { userId },
        },
      },
      _count: { id: true },
    });
    res.status(200).json({ unreadCounts });
  } catch (error) {
    console.error("Unread threads error:", error);
    res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
  }
});

export default router;

```js
// Full path: /home/luanngo/boss-dev/server/src/routes/api/chat/widget.js
import express from 'express';
import prisma from '#shared/database/prismaClient.js';
import withHandler from '#shared/utils/withHandler.js';

const router = express.Router();

const addCurrentUserPinState = (chat, userId) => {
    const taggedUsers = Array.isArray(chat?.taggedUsers) ? chat.taggedUsers : [];
    const isTaggedForCurrentUser = taggedUsers.some((tag) => tag.userId === userId);

    return {
        ...chat,
        isPinnedForCurrentUser: Boolean(chat?.isPinned || isTaggedForCurrentUser),
    };
};

const getWidgetData = async (req, res) => {
    const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;
    const organizationId = req.user.organizationId;
    const now = new Date();

    try {
        // 1. Get Pinned Chats that the user hasn't dismissed
        const pinnedChats = await prisma.chat.findMany({
            where: {
                OR: [
                    { isPinned: true },
                    { taggedUsers: { some: { userId } } },
                ],
                chatRoom: {
                    organizationId,
                    OR: [
                        { isPrivate: false },
                        { participants: { some: { id: userId } } }
                    ]
                },
                dismissedBy: {
                    none: { userId }
                }
            },
            include: {
                sender: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
                chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
                thread: { select: { id: true, title: true } },
                taggedUsers: {
                    where: { userId },
                    select: {
                        userId: true,
                        user: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
                    },
                },
            },
            orderBy: { updatedAt: 'desc' },
            take: 5,
        });

        // 2. Get unread Important Chats
        const importantChats = await prisma.chat.findMany({
            where: {
                isImportant: true,
                chatRoom: {
                    organizationId,
                    OR: [
                        { isPrivate: false },
                        { participants: { some: { id: userId } } },
                    ],
                },
                OR: [
                    { importantExpiresAt: null },
                    { importantExpiresAt: { gt: now } },
                ],
                dismissedBy: {
                    none: { userId },
                },
            },
            include: {
                sender: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
                chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
                thread: { select: { id: true, title: true } },
            },
            orderBy: { updatedAt: 'desc' },
            take: 5,
        });
        
        const excludedIds = [
            ...pinnedChats.map(c => c.id),
            ...importantChats.map(c => c.id)
        ];

        // 3. Get the most recent chats, excluding those already fetched
        const recentChats = await prisma.chat.findMany({
            where: {
                id: {
                    notIn: excludedIds,
                },
                chatRoom: {
                    organizationId,
                    OR: [
                        { isPrivate: false },
                        { participants: { some: { id: userId } } }
                    ]
                }
            },
            include: {
                sender: { select: { id: true, username: true } },
                chatRoom: { select: { id: true, name: true } },
                thread: { select: { id: true, title: true } },
            },
            orderBy: { updatedAt: 'desc' },
            take: 10,
        });

        res.status(200).json({
            pinnedChats: pinnedChats.map((chat) => addCurrentUserPinState(chat, userId)),
            importantChats,
            recentChats,
        });

    } catch (error) {
        console.error("Get Chat Widget Data Error:", error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
    }
};

const dismissChat = async (req, res) => {
    const { chatId } = req.params;
    const userId = req.user.id || req.user.userId;;

    try {
        // Use upsert to create a dismissal record if it doesn't exist.
        await prisma.userDismissedChat.upsert({
            where: { userId_chatId: { userId, chatId } },
            update: {},
            create: {
                userId,
                chatId,
            }
        });
        
        res.status(200).json({ message: "Chat dismissed for user." });
    } catch (error) {
        // Handle cases where the chat might not exist
        if (error.code === 'P2003') { 
             return res.status(404).json({ error: "Chat not found." });
        }
        console.error("Dismiss Chat Error:", error);
        res.status(500).json({ error: "Internal server error." });
    }
};


router.get('/', withHandler({
    handler: getWidgetData,
    allowedMethods: ['GET']
}));

router.put('/:chatId/dismiss', withHandler({
    handler: dismissChat,
    allowedMethods: ['PUT']
}));

export default router;

```
